Al-Suddi said concerning {And We brought him near, conversing intimately}: he said, he was brought into the heaven and was spoken to. And something similar is reported from Mujahid.

Abd al-Razzaq said, from Ma'mar, from Qatadah, concerning {And We brought him near, conversing intimately}: he said, he was saved (naja) through his truthfulness.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Abd al-Jabbar ibn 'Asim told us, Muhammad ibn Salamah al-Harrani told us, from Abu al-Wasl, from Shahr ibn Hawshab, from 'Amr ibn Ma'd Yakrib, who said: When Allah brought Musa near in intimate conversation at Mount Sinai, He said: "O Musa, when I create for you a grateful heart, a remembering tongue, and a wife who helps toward good, I have not withheld from you anything of good, and whoever I withhold this from, I have not opened for him anything of good."

His saying: {And We granted him from Our mercy his brother Harun as a prophet}, that is: We answered his request and his intercession on behalf of his brother, and so We made him a prophet, as He said in another verse: {And my brother Harun, he is more eloquent of tongue than me, so send him with me as a support, confirming me; indeed I fear that they will call me a liar} [al-Qasas: 34], and He said: {You have been granted your request, O Musa} [Ta Ha: 36], and He said: {So send for Harun. And they have a charge against me, so I fear that they will kill me} [al-Shu'ara: 13-14]. For this reason some of the early scholars said: No one has ever interceded for anyone in this world with an intercession greater than the intercession of Musa for Harun, that he become a prophet. Allah the Exalted said: {And We granted him from Our mercy his brother Harun as a prophet}.

Ibn Jarir said: Ya'qub told us, Ibn 'Ulayyah told us, from Dawud, from 'Ikrimah, who said: Ibn 'Abbas said, regarding His saying {And We granted him from Our mercy his brother Harun as a prophet}: he said, Harun was older than Musa, but what is meant is that He granted him his prophethood.

Ibn Abi Hatim also mentioned it in mu'allaq (suspended) form, from Ya'qub, that is, Ibn Ibrahim al-Dawraqi, with the same content.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْخَلِيلَ وَأَثْنَى عَلَيْهِ، عَطَفَ بِذِكْرِ الْكَلِيمِ، فَقَالَ: ﴿وَاذْكُرْ فِي الْكِتَابِ مُوسَى إِنَّهُ كَانَ مُخْلَصًا﴾ قَرَأَ بَعْضُهُمْ بِكَسْرِ اللَّامِ، مِنَ الْإِخْلَاصِ فِي الْعِبَادَةِ.

قَالَ الثَّوْرِيُّ ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ بْنِ رُفَيع ، عَنْ أَبِي لُبَابَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ الْحَوَارِيُّونَ: يَا رُوحَ اللَّهِ، أَخْبِرْنَا عَنِ الْمُخْلِصِ لِلَّهِ. قَالَ: الَّذِي يَعْمَلُ لِلَّهِ، لَا يُحِبُّ أَنْ يَحْمَدَهُ النَّاسُ.

وَقَرَأَ الْآخَرُونَ بِفَتْحِهَا، بِمَعْنَى أَنَّهُ كَانَ مُصْطَفًى، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿إِنِّي اصْطَفَيْتُكَ عَلَى النَّاسِ﴾ [الْأَعْرَافِ: ١٤٤] .

﴿وَكَانَ رَسُولا نَبِيًّا﴾ ، جُمِع لَهُ بَيْنَ الْوَصْفَيْنِ، فَإِنَّهُ كَانَ مِنَ الْمُرْسَلِينَ الْكِبَارِ أُولِي الْعَزْمِ الْخَمْسَةِ، وَهُمْ: نُوحٌ وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ، وَمُوسَى، وَعِيسَى، وَمُحَمَّدٌ، صَلَوَاتُ اللَّهِ وَسَلَامُهُ عَلَيْهِمْ وَعَلَى سَائِرِ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ أَجْمَعِينَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَنَادَيْنَاهُ مِنْ جَانِبِ الطُّورِ﴾ أَيِ: الْجَبَلِ ﴿الأيْمَنِ﴾ أَيْ: مِنْ جَانِبِهِ الْأَيْمَنِ مِنْ مُوسَى حِينَ ذَهَبَ يَبْتَغِي مِنْ تِلْكَ النَّارِ جَذْوَةً، رَآهَا تَلُوحُ فَقَصَدَهَا، فَوَجَدَهَا فِي جَانِبِ الطُّوْرِ الْأَيْمَنِ مِنْهُ ، عِنْدَ شَاطِئِ الْوَادِي. فَكَلَّمَهُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى، نَادَاهُ وَقَرَّبَهُ وَنَاجَاهُ . قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ بَشَّارٍ ، حَدَّثَنَا يَحْيَى -هُوَ الْقَطَّانُ-حَدَّثَنَا سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ عَطَاءِ بْنِ السَّائِبِ ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جبير، عن ابن عباس: ﴿وَقَرَّبْنَاهُ نَجِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: أُدْنِيَ حَتَّى سَمِعَ صَرِيفَ القلم.

وَهَكَذَا قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَأَبُو الْعَالِيَةِ، وَغَيْرُهُمْ. يَعْنُونَ صَرِيفَ الْقَلَمِ بِكِتَابَةِ التَّوْرَاةِ.

وَقَالَ السُّدِّيُّ: ﴿وَقَرَّبْنَاهُ نَجِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: أُدْخِلَ فِي السَّمَاءِ فَكُلِّمَ، وَعَنْ مجاهد نَحْوَهُ.

وَقَالَ عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، عَنْ مَعْمَر، عَنْ قَتَادَةَ: ﴿وَقَرَّبْنَاهُ نَجِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: نَجَا بِصِدْقِهِ 

قَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الْجَبَّارِ بْنُ عَاصِمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ سَلَمَةَ الْحَرَّانِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي الْوَصْلِ، عَنْ شَهْرِ بْنِ حَوْشَب، عن عمرو بن معد يكرب قَالَ: لَمَّا قَرَّبَ اللَّهُ مُوسَى نَجِيًّا بِطُورِ سَيْنَاءَ، قَالَ: يَا مُوسَى، إِذَا خَلَقْتُ لَكَ قَلْبًا شَاكِرًا، وَلِسَانًا ذَاكِرًا، وَزَوْجَةً تُعِينُ عَلَى الْخَيْرِ، فَلَمْ أُخَزِّنْ عَنْكَ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ شَيْئًا، وَمَنْ أُخَزِّنُ عَنْهُ هَذَا فَلَمْ أَفْتَحْ لَهُ مِنَ الْخَيْرِ شَيْئًا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ مِنْ رَحْمَتِنَا أَخَاهُ هَارُونَ نَبِيًّا﴾ أَيْ: وَأَجَبْنَا سُؤَالَهُ وَشَفَاعَتَهُ فِي أَخِيهِ، فَجَعَلْنَاهُ نَبِيًّا، كَمَا قَالَ فِي الْآيَةِ الْأُخْرَى: ﴿وَأَخِي هَارُونُ هُوَ أَفْصَحُ مِنِّي لِسَانًا فَأَرْسِلْهُ مَعِيَ رِدْءًا يُصَدِّقُنِي إِنِّي أَخَافُ أَنْ يُكَذِّبُونِ﴾ [الْقَصَصِ: ٣٤] ، وَقَالَ : ﴿قَدْ أُوتِيتَ سُؤْلَكَ يَا مُوسَى﴾ [طَهَ: ٣٦] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿فَأَرْسِلْ إِلَى هَارُونَ. وَلَهُمْ عَلَيَّ ذَنْبٌ فَأَخَافُ أَنْ يَقْتُلُونِ﴾ [الشُّعَرَاءِ: ١٣، ١٤] ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ بَعْضُ السَّلَفِ: مَا شُفِّعَ أَحَدٌ فِي أَحَدٍ شَفَاعَةً فِي الدُّنْيَا أَعْظَمُ مِنْ شَفَاعَةِ مُوسَى فِي هَارُونَ أَنْ يَكُونَ نَبِيًّا، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ مِنْ رَحْمَتِنَا أَخَاهُ هَارُونَ نَبِيًّا﴾ .

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ، حَدَّثَنَا ابْنُ عُلَيَّة، عَنْ دَاوُدَ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ: قَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ مِنْ رَحْمَتِنَا أَخَاهُ هَارُونَ نَبِيًّا﴾ ، قَالَ: كَانَ هَارُونُ أَكْبَرَ مِنْ مُوسَى، وَلَكِنْ أَرَادَ: وَهَبَ لَهُ نُبُوَّتَهُ.

وَقَدْ ذَكَرَهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مُعَلَّقًا، عَنْ يَعْقُوبَ وَهُوَ ابْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الدَّوْرَقِيُّ، بِهِ.

---

## 19:54-55 — verses 54-55 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is praise from God, Exalted is He, of Ismail son of Ibrahim the Khalil (peace be upon them both), who is the father of all the Arabs of the Hijaz, in that {he was true to his promise}.

Ibn Jurayj said: He never made a promise to his Lord without fulfilling it, meaning that he never bound himself to an act of worship by a vow without carrying it out and giving it its full due.

Ibn Jarir said: Yunus narrated to me, Ibn Wahb informed us, Amr ibn al-Harith informed me, that Sahl ibn Aqil narrated to him, that Ismail the Prophet ﷺ promised a man that he would come to him at a certain place. He came, but the man forgot. So Ismail remained there through the day and spent the night, until the man came the next day and said, "Have you not left this place?" He said, "No." The man said, "I had forgotten." Ismail said, "I would not have left until you came to me." That is why {he was true to his promise}.

Sufyan al-Thawri said: It has reached me that he remained in that place waiting for him for a full year until he came to him.

Ibn Shawdhab said: It has reached me that he took that spot as a dwelling place.

Abu Dawud related in his Sunan, and Abu Bakr Muhammad ibn Ja'far al-Kharaiti in his book "Makarim al-Akhlaq," through the route of Ibrahim ibn Tahman, from Abdullah ibn Maysara, from Abd al-Karim, meaning Ibn Abdullah ibn Shaqiq, from his father, from Abdullah ibn Abi al-Hamsa, who said: I made a transaction with the Messenger of God ﷺ before he was sent as a prophet, and a remaining amount was still owed to him by me. I promised him that I would bring it to him at that same place. He said: But I forgot, that day and the next, and I came to him on the third day, and he was still in that same place. He said to me, "Young man, you have caused me hardship. I have been here for three days waiting for you." This is the wording of al-Kharaiti, who cited several good reports on this matter.

Ibn Mandah, Abu Abdullah, related it in his book "Ma'rifat al-Sahaba," with his chain, from Ibrahim ibn Tahman, from Budayl ibn Maysara, from Abd al-Karim, with the same content.

Some of them said: He was called {true to his promise} only because he said to his father, {You will find me, if God wills, among the patient} [al-Saffat: 102], and he was indeed true to that.

So truthfulness in fulfilling a promise is among the praiseworthy qualities, just as breaking it is among the blameworthy ones. God, Exalted is He, said: {O you who believe, why do you say what you do not do? It is greatly hateful in the sight of God that you say what you do not do} [al-Saff: 2-3]. And the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "The sign of the hypocrite is three: when he speaks he lies, when he promises he breaks his promise, and when he is entrusted he betrays the trust."

Since these are the qualities of the hypocrites, being characterized by their opposite is among the qualities of the believers. This is why God praised His servant and messenger Ismail for being true to his promise. Likewise, the Messenger of God ﷺ was also true to his promise. He never promised anyone anything without fulfilling it for him. He praised Abu al-As ibn al-Rabi', the husband of his daughter Zaynab, saying, "He spoke to me and was truthful with me, and he promised me and was faithful to me." When the Prophet ﷺ passed away, the caliph Abu Bakr al-Siddiq said, "Whoever has a promise or a debt owed to him by the Messenger of God ﷺ, let him come to me and I will fulfill it for him." Jabir ibn Abdullah came to him and said, "The Messenger of God ﷺ had said, 'If the wealth of Bahrain comes, I will give you this much, and this much, and this much,'" meaning two handfuls. When the wealth of Bahrain came, al-Siddiq ordered Jabir, and he scooped with both his hands from the wealth, then he ordered him to count it, and it turned out to be five hundred dirhams, so he gave him twice that amount along with it.

As for His saying, {and he was a messenger, a prophet}, in this is an indication of the honor of Ismail over his brother Ishaq, for Ishaq was described only with prophethood, while Ismail was described with both prophethood and messengership. It is established in Sahih Muslim that the Messenger of God ﷺ said, "Indeed God chose from the children of Ibrahim, Ismail..." and he mentioned the rest of the hadith, which indicates the soundness of what we have said.

As for His saying, {And he used to enjoin upon his family prayer and zakat, and he was pleasing in the sight of his Lord}, this too is part of the beautiful praise, the praiseworthy quality, and the sound character trait, in that he was persistent in obedience to his Lord and commanded it to his family, just as God, Exalted is He, said to His Messenger: {And enjoin prayer upon your family and be steadfast therein. We do not ask you for provision; We provide for you, and the good end is for righteousness} [Ta Ha: 132]. And God, Exalted is He, said: {O you who believe, protect yourselves and your families from a fire whose fuel is people and stones, over which are angels harsh and severe} [al-Tahrim: 6], meaning: command them to do good and forbid them from evil, and do not leave them neglected so that the fire consumes them on the Day of Resurrection.

It has come in a hadith, from Abu Hurayrah, who said: The Messenger of God ﷺ said, "May God have mercy on a man who rises at night and prays, and wakes his wife, and if she refuses he sprinkles water on her face. May God have mercy on a woman who rises at night and prays, and wakes her husband, and if he refuses she sprinkles water on his face." Reported by Abu Dawud and Ibn Majah.

And from Abu Sa'id and Abu Hurayrah, may God be pleased with them both, from the Prophet ﷺ, who said: "If a man wakes at night and wakes his wife, and they pray two rak'ahs together, they are recorded among the men who remember God much and the women who remember Him much." Reported by Abu Dawud, al-Nasa'i, and Ibn Majah, and the wording is his.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

هَذَا ثَنَاءٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى عَلَى إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْخَلِيلِ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ، وَهُوَ وَالِدُ عَرَبِ الْحِجَازِ كُلِّهِمْ بِأَنَّهُ ﴿كَانَ صَادِقَ الْوَعْدِ﴾

قَالَ ابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ: لَمْ يَعدْ رَبَّهُ عِدَةً إِلَّا أَنْجَزَهَا، يَعْنِي: مَا الْتَزَمَ قَطُّ عِبَادَةً بِنَذْرٍ إِلَّا قَامَ بِهَا، وَوَفَّاهَا حَقَّهَا.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي يُونُسُ، أَنْبَأَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي عَمْرُو بْنُ الْحَارِثِ، أَنَّ سَهْلَ بْنَ عَقِيلٍ حَدَّثَهُ، أَنَّ إِسْمَاعِيلَ النَّبِيَّ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَعَدَ رَجُلًا مَكَانًا أَنْ يَأْتِيَهُ، فَجَاءَ وَنَسِيَ الرَّجُلُ، فَظَلَّ بِهِ إِسْمَاعِيلُ وَبَاتَ حَتَّى جَاءَ الرَّجُلُ مِنَ الْغَدِ، فَقَالَ: مَا بَرِحْتَ مِنْ هَاهُنَا؟ قَالَ: لَا. قَالَ: إِنِّي نَسِيتُ. قَالَ: لَمْ أَكُنْ لِأَبْرَحَ حَتَّى تَأْتِيَنِي. فلذلك ﴿كَانَ صَادِقَ الْوَعْدِ﴾ .

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّهُ أَقَامَ فِي ذَلِكَ الْمَكَانِ يَنْتَظِرُهُ حَوْلًا حَتَّى جَاءَهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ شَوْذَب: بَلَغَنِي أَنَّهُ اتَّخَذَ ذَلِكَ الْمَوْضِعَ سَكَنًا.

وَقَدْ رَوَى أَبُو دَاوُدَ فِي سُنَنِهِ، وَأَبُو بَكْرٍ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ جَعْفَرٍ الْخَرَائِطِيُّ فِي كِتَابِهِ "مَكَارِمِ الْأَخْلَاقِ" مِنْ طَرِيقِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ طَهْمَان، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَيْسَرة، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْكَرِيمِ -يَعْنِي: ابْنَ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ شَقيق-عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ أَبِي الْحَمْسَاءِ قَالَ: بَايَعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَبْلَ أَنْ يُبْعَثَ فَبَقِيَتْ لَهُ عَلَيَّ بَقِيَّةٌ، فَوَعَدْتُهُ أَنْ آتِيَهُ بِهَا فِي مَكَانِهِ ذَلِكَ، قَالَ: فَنَسِيتُ يَوْمِي وَالْغَدَ، فَأَتَيْتُهُ فِي الْيَوْمِ الثَّالِثِ وَهُوَ فِي مَكَانِهِ ذَلِكَ، فَقَالَ لِي: "يَا فَتَى، لَقَدْ شَقَقْتَ عَلَيَّ، أَنَا هَاهُنَا مُنْذُ ثَلَاثٍ أَنْتَظِرُكَ" لَفْظُ الْخَرَائِطِيِّ ، وَسَاقَ آثَارًا حَسَنَةً فِي ذَلِكَ.

وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ مَنْده أَبُو عَبْدِ اللَّهِ فِي كِتَابِ "مَعْرِفَةِ الصَّحَابَةِ"، بِإِسْنَادِهِ عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ طَهْمَان، عَنْ بُدَيْل بْنِ مَيْسَرَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ الْكَرِيمِ، بِهِ .

وَقَالَ بَعْضُهُمْ: إِنَّمَا قِيلَ لَهُ: ﴿صَادِقَ الْوَعْدِ﴾ ؛ لِأَنَّهُ قَالَ لِأَبِيهِ: ﴿سَتَجِدُنِي إِنْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ مِنَ الصَّابِرِينَ﴾ [الصَّافَّاتِ: ١٠٢] ، فَصَدَقَ فِي ذَلِكَ.

فَصِدْقُ الْوَعْدِ مِنَ الصِّفَاتِ الْحَمِيدَةِ، كَمَا أَنَّ خُلْفَه مِنَ الصِّفَاتِ الذَّمِيمَةِ، قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لِمَ تَقُولُونَ مَا لَا تَفْعَلُونَ كَبُرَ مَقْتًا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ أَنْ تَقُولُوا مَا لَا تَفْعَلُونَ﴾ [الصَّفِّ: ٢، ٣] وَقَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "آيَةُ الْمُنَافِقِ ثَلَاثٌ: إِذَا حَدَّثَ كَذَبَ، وَإِذَا وَعَدَ أَخْلَفَ، وَإِذَا اؤْتُمِنَ خَانَ" 

وَلَمَّا كَانَتْ هَذِهِ صِفَاتُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ، كَانَ التَّلَبُّسُ بِضِدِّهَا مِنْ صِفَاتِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، وَلِهَذَا أَثْنَى اللَّهُ عَلَى عَبْدِهِ وَرَسُولِهِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بِصِدْقِ الْوَعْدِ، وَكَذَلِكَ كَانَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ صَادِقَ الْوَعْدِ أَيْضًا، لَا يَعِدُ أَحَدًا شَيْئًا إِلَّا وَفَّى لَهُ بِهِ، وَقَدْ أَثْنَى عَلَى أَبِي الْعَاصِ بْنِ الرَّبِيعِ زَوْجِ ابْنَتِهِ زَيْنَبَ، فَقَالَ: "حَدَّثَنِي فَصَدَقَنِي، وَوَعَدَنِي فَوَفَى لِي" . وَلَمَّا تُوُفِّيَ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ قَالَ الْخَلِيفَةُ أَبُو بَكْرٍ الصِّدِّيقُ: مَنْ كَانَ لَهُ عِنْدَ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ عدَةٌ أَوْ دَيْن فَلْيَأْتِنِي أُنْجِزْ لَهُ، فَجَاءَهُ جَابِرُ بْنُ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ، فَقَالَ: إِنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ كَانَ قَالَ: "لَوْ جَاءَ مَالُ الْبَحْرَيْنِ أَعْطَيْتُكَ هَكَذَا وَهَكَذَا وَهَكَذَا"، يَعْنِي: مِلْءَ كَفَّيْهِ، فَلَمَّا جَاءَ مَالُ الْبَحْرِينِ أَمَرَ الصِّدِّيقُ جَابِرًا، فَغَرَفَ بِيَدَيْهِ مِنَ الْمَالِ، ثُمَّ أَمَرَهُ بِعَدّه، فَإِذَا هُوَ خَمْسُمِائَةِ دِرْهَمٍ، فَأَعْطَاهُ مِثْلَيْهَا مَعَهَا 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَانَ رَسُولا نَبِيًّا﴾ فِي هَذَا دَلَالَةٌ عَلَى شَرَفِ إِسْمَاعِيلَ عَلَى أَخِيهِ إِسْحَاقَ؛ لِأَنَّهُ إنما وُصِفَ بِالنُّبُوَّةِ فَقَطْ، وَإِسْمَاعِيلُ وُصِفَ بِالنُّبُوَّةِ وَالرِّسَالَةِ. وَقَدْ ثَبَتَ فِي صَحِيحِ مُسْلِمٍ أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِنَّ اللَّهَ اصْطَفَى مِنْ وَلَدِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ إِسْمَاعِيلَ ... " وَذَكَرَ تَمَامَ الْحَدِيثِ، فَدَلَّ عَلَى صِحَّةِ مَا قُلْنَاهُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَكَانَ يَأْمُرُ أَهْلَهُ بِالصَّلاةِ وَالزَّكَاةِ وَكَانَ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِ مَرْضِيًّا﴾ : هَذَا أَيْضًا مِنَ الثَّنَاءِ الْجَمِيلِ، وَالصِّفَةِ الْحَمِيدَةِ، وَالْخِلَّةِ السَّدِيدَةِ ، حَيْثُ كَانَ مُثَابِرًا عَلَى طَاعَةِ رَبِّهِ آمِرًا بِهَا لِأَهْلِهِ ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى لِرَسُولِهِ: ﴿وَأْمُرْ أَهْلَكَ بِالصَّلاةِ وَاصْطَبِرْ عَلَيْهَا لَا نَسْأَلُكَ رِزْقًا نَحْنُ نَرْزُقُكَ وَالْعَاقِبَةُ لِلتَّقْوَى﴾ [طه: ١٣٢] ، وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا قُوا أَنْفُسَكُمْ وَأَهْلِيكُمْ نَارًا وَقُودُهَا النَّاسُ وَالْحِجَارَةُ عَلَيْهَا مَلائِكَةٌ غِلاظٌ شِدَادٌ﴾ الْآيَةَ [التَّحْرِيمِ: ٦] أَيْ: مُرُوهُمْ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ، وَانْهَوْهُمْ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ، وَلَا تَدَعُوهُمْ هَمْلًا فَتَأْكُلَهُمُ النَّارُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ، وَقَدْ جَاءَ فِي الْحَدِيثِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "رَحِمَ اللَّهُ رَجُلًا قَامَ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ فَصَلَّى، وَأَيْقَظَ امْرَأَتَهُ، فَإِنْ أَبَتْ نَضَح فِي وَجْهِهَا الْمَاءَ، رَحِمَ اللَّهُ امْرَأَةً قَامَتْ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ فَصَلَّتْ، وَأَيْقَظَتْ زَوْجَهَا، فَإِنْ أَبَى نَضَحَتْ فِي وَجْهِهِ الْمَاءَ" أَخْرَجَهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ .

وَعَنْ أَبِي سَعِيدٍ، وَأَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمَا، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "إِذَا اسْتَيْقَظَ الرَّجُلُ مِنَ اللَّيْلِ وَأَيْقَظَ امْرَأَتَهُ، فَصَلَّيَا رَكْعَتَيْنِ، كُتِبَا مِنَ الذَّاكِرِينَ اللَّهَ كَثِيرًا وَالذَّاكِرَاتِ". رَوَاهُ أَبُو دَاوُدَ، وَالنَّسَائِيُّ، وَابْنُ مَاجَهْ، وَاللَّفْظُ لَهُ .

---

## 19:56-57 — verses 56-57 (shared commentary)

### Translation

This is the mention of Idris (peace be upon him) with praise for him, that he was truthful and a prophet, and that God raised him to a high station. It has already been established in the sound hadith that the Messenger of God ﷺ passed by him on the night of the Night Journey while he was in the fourth heaven.

Ibn Jarir has related here a gharib (singular) and remarkable report. He said: Yunus ibn Abd al-A'la related to me, Ibn Wahb informed us, Jarir ibn Hazim informed me, from Sulayman al-A'mash, from Shamir ibn Atiyyah, from Hilal ibn Yasaf, who said: Ibn Abbas asked Ka'b, while I was present, saying to him: What is the meaning of God's, Mighty and Majestic, saying about Idris {and We raised him to a high station}? Ka'b said: As for Idris, God revealed to him: "I raise up for you each day the equivalent of the deeds of all the children of Adam together." So he wished to increase his deeds, and a friend of his among the angels came to him and said: "God has revealed to me such and such, so speak on my behalf to the Angel of Death, that he might delay me so I may increase my deeds." So the angel carried him between his wings and ascended with him to heaven. When they reached the fourth heaven, the Angel of Death met them descending. Idris's friend spoke to the Angel of Death about what Idris had asked him regarding. The Angel of Death said: "And where is Idris?" He replied: "He is here upon my back." The Angel of Death said: "How astonishing! I was sent and told: 'Take the soul of Idris in the fourth heaven.' And I kept saying: 'How can I take his soul in the fourth heaven when he is on earth?'" So he took his soul there. That is the meaning of God's saying: {and We raised him to a high station}.

This is among the reports of Ka'b al-Ahbar drawn from the Isra'iliyyat (Israelite-derived narrations), and in some of it there is nakarah (objectionable strangeness). And God knows best.

Ibn Abi Hatim related it by another route, from Ibn Abbas, that he asked Ka'b, and he mentioned something similar to what preceded, except that he said the angel said to that other angel: "Would you ask him," meaning the Angel of Death, "how much remains of my term of life, so that I may increase in deeds?" And he mentioned the rest of it. In it, when he asked him about what remained of his term, he said: "I do not know, until I look." Then he looked and said: "You are asking me about a man who has nothing left of his life but the blink of an eye." So the angel looked under his wing at Idris, and there he was, already taken (peace be upon him), while the angel bearing him was unaware of it.

Then he related it by another route from Ibn Abbas: that Idris was a tailor, and he would never push in a needle without saying "Glory be to God (Subhan Allah)." So when evening came, there was no one on earth with more excellent deeds than he. And he mentioned the rest of it as in the previous report, or something similar to it.

Ibn Abi Najih said, from Mujahid, concerning His saying {and We raised him to a high station}: he said: Idris was raised up and did not die, just as Jesus was raised up.

Sufyan said, from Mansur, from Mujahid: {and We raised him to a high station}, he said: he was raised to the fourth heaven.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas: {and We raised him to a high station}, he said: he was raised to the sixth heaven and died there. And likewise said al-Dahhak ibn Muzahim.

Al-Hasan and others said, concerning His saying {and We raised him to a high station}: he said: it means Paradise.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

وَهَذَا ذِكْرُ إِدْرِيسَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، بِالثَّنَاءِ عَلَيْهِ، بِأَنَّهُ كَانَ صِدِّيقًا نَبِيًّا، وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ رَفَعَهُ مَكَانًا عَلِيًّا. وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ فِي الصَّحِيحِ: أَنَّ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ صَلَّى اللَّهُ عليه وسلم مَرَّ بِهِ فِي لَيْلَةِ الْإِسْرَاءِ وَهُوَ فِي السَّمَاءِ الرَّابِعَةِ.

وَقَدْ رَوَى ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ هَاهُنَا أَثَرًا غَرِيبًا عَجِيبًا، فَقَالَ: حَدَّثَنِي يُونُسُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الْأَعْلَى، أَنْبَأَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي جَرِيرُ بْنُ حَازِمٍ، عَنْ سُلَيْمَانَ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ شَمِر بْنِ عَطِيَّةَ، عَنْ هِلَالِ بْنِ يَسَافٍ قَالَ: سَأَلَ ابْنُ عَبَّاسٍ كَعْبًا، وَأَنَا حَاضِرٌ، فَقَالَ لَهُ: مَا قَوْلُ اللَّهِ -عَزَّ وَجَلَّ-لِإِدْرِيسَ: ﴿وَرَفَعْنَاهُ مَكَانًا عَلِيًّا﴾ فَقَالَ كَعْبٌ: أَمَّا إِدْرِيسُ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ أَوْحَى إِلَيْهِ أَنِّي أَرْفَعُ لَكَ كُلَّ يَوْمٍ مِثْلَ عَمَلِ جَمِيعِ بَنِي آدَمَ، فَأَحَبَّ أَنْ يَزْدَادَ عَمَلًا فَأَتَاهُ خَلِيلٌ لَهُ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ فَقَالَ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ أَوْحَى إِلَيَّ كَذَا وَكَذَا، فَكَلِّمْ لِي مَلَكَ الْمَوْتِ، فَلْيؤخرني حَتَّى أَزْدَادَ عَمَلًا فَحَمَلَهُ بَيْنَ جَنَاحَيْهِ، حَتَّى صَعِدَ بِهِ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ، فَلَمَّا كَانَ فِي السَّمَاءِ الرَّابِعَةِ تَلَقَّاهُمْ مَلَك الْمَوْتِ مُنْحَدِرًا، فَكَلَّمَ مَلَكَ الْمَوْتِ فِي الَّذِي كَلَّمَهُ فِيهِ إِدْرِيسُ، فَقَالَ: وَأَيْنَ إِدْرِيسُ؟ فَقَالَ: هُوَ ذَا عَلَى ظَهْرِي. قَالَ مَلَكُ الْمَوْتِ: فَالْعَجَبُ! بُعِثْتُ وَقِيلَ لي: اقبض روح إدريس فِي السَّمَاءِ الرَّابِعَةِ". فَجَعَلْتُ أَقُولُ: كَيْفَ أَقْبِضُ رُوحَهُ فِي السَّمَاءِ الرَّابِعَةِ، وَهُوَ فِي الْأَرْضِ؟ فَقَبَضَ رُوْحَهُ هُنَاكَ، فَذَلِكَ قَوْلُ اللَّهِ: ﴿وَرَفَعْنَاهُ مَكَانًا عَلِيًّا﴾ .

هَذَا مِنْ أَخْبَارِ كَعْبِ الْأَحْبَارِ الْإِسْرَائِيلِيَّاتِ، وَفِي بَعْضِهِ نَكَارَةٌ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

وَقَدْ رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّهُ سَأَلَ كَعْبًا، فَذَكَرَ نَحْوَ مَا تَقَدَّمَ، غَيْرَ أَنَّهُ قَالَ لِذَلِكَ الْمَلَكِ: هَلْ لَكَ أَنْ تَسْأَلَهُ -يَعْنِي: مَلَكَ الْمَوْتِ-كَمْ بَقِيَ مِنْ أَجَلِي لِكَيْ أَزْدَادَ مِنَ الْعَمَلِ وَذَكَرَ بَاقِيَهُ ، وَفِيهِ: أَنَّهُ لَمَّا سَأَلَهُ عَمَّا بَقِيَ مِنْ أَجْلِهِ، قَالَ : لَا أَدْرِي حَتَّى أَنْظُرَ، ثُمَّ نَظَرَ، قَالَ: إِنَّكَ تَسْأَلُنِي عَنْ رَجُلٍ مَا بَقِيَ مِنْ عُمْرِهِ إِلَّا طَرْفَةُ عَيْنٍ، فَنَظَرَ الْمَلَكُ تَحْتَ جَنَاحِهِ إِلَى إِدْرِيسَ، فَإِذَا هُوَ قَدْ قُبِضَ، عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ، وَهُوَ لَا يَشْعُرُ بِهِ.

ثُمَّ رَوَاهُ مِنْ وَجْهٍ آخَرَ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: أَنَّ إِدْرِيسَ كَانَ خَيَّاطًا، فَكَانَ لَا يَغْرِزُ إِبْرَةً إِلَّا قَالَ: "سُبْحَانَ اللَّهِ"، فَكَانَ يُمْسِي حِينَ يُمْسِي وَلَيْسَ فِي الْأَرْضِ أَحَدٌ أَفْضَلَ عَمَلًا مِنْهُ. وَذَكَرَ بَقِيَّتَهُ كَالَّذِي قَبْلَهُ، أَوْ نَحْوَهُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَرَفَعْنَاهُ مَكَانًا عَلِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: إِدْرِيسُ رُفِعَ وَلَمْ يَمُتْ، كَمَا رُفِعَ عِيسَى.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ، عَنْ مَنْصُورٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿وَرَفَعْنَاهُ مَكَانًا عَلِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: [رُفِعَ إِلَى] السَّمَاءِ الرَّابِعَةِ.

وَقَالَ الْعَوْفِيُّ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَرَفَعْنَاهُ مَكَانًا عَلِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: رُفِعَ إِلَى السَّمَاءِ السَّادِسَةِ فَمَاتَ بِهَا. وَهَكَذَا قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ بْنُ مُزَاحم.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ، وَغَيْرُهُ، فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَرَفَعْنَاهُ مَكَانًا عَلِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: الْجَنَّةُ.

---

## 19:58 — verse 58

### Translation

The Almighty says: these are the prophets, and what is meant is not [these] mentioned in this surah alone, but rather the category of prophets (peace be upon them) in general. He moved on from mentioning specific individuals to mentioning the category as a whole: {those upon whom Allah bestowed favor, from the prophets, from the offspring of Adam} to the end of the verse.

Al-Suddi and Ibn Jarir, may Allah have mercy on him, said: [the one meant by "from the offspring of Adam" is Idris, and the one meant by "from the offspring of those We carried with Nuh" is Ibrahim], and the one meant by "from the offspring of Ibrahim" is Ishaq, Ya'qub, and Isma'il, and the one meant by "from the offspring of Israel" is Musa, Harun, Zakariyya, Yahya, and 'Isa son of Maryam.

Ibn Jarir said: for this reason he distinguished their lineages, even though Adam gathers all of them together, because among them is one who is not from the descendants of those who were with Nuh in the ark, namely Idris, for he was an ancestor of Nuh.

I say: this is the more apparent view, that Idris is within the line of descent leading to Nuh (peace be upon them both). It has also been said that he is among the prophets of the Children of Israel, taking this from the hadith of the Night Journey (al-Isra), where, in his greeting to the Prophet ﷺ, he said: "Welcome to the righteous prophet and the righteous brother," and he did not say "the righteous son," as Adam and Ibrahim (peace be upon them) said.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] from 'Abdullah ibn Muhammad, that Idris was earlier than Nuh. Allah sent him to his people and commanded them to say "There is no god but Allah," and to do as they wished otherwise, but they refused, so Allah, Mighty and Majestic, destroyed them.

[Among the things that support the view that what is meant by this verse is the category of prophets in general is that it resembles what Allah says in Surat al-An'am]: {And that is Our argument which We gave to Ibrahim against his people. We raise in degrees whom We will. Indeed your Lord is Wise, Knowing. And We bestowed upon him Ishaq and Ya'qub; each We guided. And Nuh We guided before, and among his descendants, Dawud, Sulayman, Ayyub, Yusuf, Musa, and Harun. Thus do We reward the doers of good. And Zakariyya, Yahya, 'Isa, and Ilyas; each was among the righteous. And Isma'il, al-Yasa', Yunus, and Lut; each We favored above the worlds. And among their fathers, their descendants, and their brothers; and We chose them and guided them to a straight path} up to His saying: {Those are the ones whom Allah has guided, so follow their guidance. Say: I do not ask you for any reward for it; it is not except a reminder for the worlds} [al-An'am 83-90]. And the Almighty says: {Of them are those We have related to you, and of them are those We have not related to you} [Ghafir: 78]. In Sahih al-Bukhari, from Mujahid, that he asked Ibn 'Abbas: is there a prostration in Surat "Sad"? He said: yes, then he recited this verse: {Those are the ones whom Allah has guided, so follow their guidance}, so your Prophet is among those commanded to follow their example. He said: and he, meaning Dawud, is among them.

Allah the Almighty says in this noble verse: {When the verses of the Most Merciful are recited to them, they fall down in prostration and weeping}, meaning: when they heard the speech of Allah containing His proofs, His signs, and His demonstrations, they prostrated to their Lord out of humility and submission, and out of praise and gratitude for the immense blessings they were in.

"Al-buki" (weeping) is the plural of "bakin" (one who weeps). For this reason the scholars agreed unanimously on the legitimacy of prostration here, following their example and walking in their path.

Sufyan al-Thawri said, from al-A'mash, from Ibrahim, from Abu Ma'mar, who said: 'Umar ibn al-Khattab, may Allah be pleased with him, recited Surat Maryam, and he prostrated, and said: this is the prostration, but where is the weeping? Meaning weeping itself.

It was narrated by Ibn Abi Hatim and Ibn Jarir, and the mention of "Abu Ma'mar" is missing from his narration as far as I have seen, and Allah knows best.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى هَؤُلَاءِ النَّبِيُّونَ -وَلَيْسَ الْمُرَادُ [هَؤُلَاءِ] الْمَذْكُورِينَ فِي هَذِهِ السُّورَةِ فَقَطْ، بَلْ جِنْسُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ، اسْتَطْرَدَ مِنْ ذِكْرِ الْأَشْخَاصِ إِلَى الْجِنْسِ - ﴿الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنَ النَّبِيِّينَ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ آدَمَ﴾ الآية.

قَالَ السُّدِّيُّ وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ: [فَالَّذِي عَنَى بِهِ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ آدَمَ: إِدْرِيسَ، وَالَّذِي عَنَى بِهِ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ مَنْ حَمَلْنَا مَعَ نُوحٍ: إِبْرَاهِيمَ] وَالَّذِي عَنَى بِهِ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ: إِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ، وَالَّذِي عَنَى بِهِ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّةِ إِسْرَائِيلَ: مُوسَى، وَهَارُونَ، وَزَكَرِيَّا وَيَحْيَى وَعِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ.

قَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: وَلِذَلِكَ فَرَّقَ أَنْسَابَهُمْ، وَإِنْ كَانَ يَجْمَعُ جَمِيعَهُمْ آدَمُ؛ لِأَنَّ فِيهِمْ مَنْ لَيْسَ مِنْ وَلَدِ مَنْ كَانَ مَعَ نُوحٍ فِي السَّفِينَةِ، وَهُوَ إِدْرِيسُ، فَإِنَّهُ جَدُّ نُوحٍ.

قُلْتُ: هَذَا هُوَ الْأَظْهَرُ أَنَّ إِدْرِيسَ فِي عَمُودِ نَسَبِ نُوحٍ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ. وَقَدْ قِيلَ: إِنَّهُ مِنْ أَنْبِيَاءِ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ، أَخْذًا مِنْ حَدِيثِ الْإِسْرَاءِ، حَيْثُ قَالَ فِي سَلَامِهِ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ: "مَرْحَبًا بِالنَّبِيِّ الصَّالِحِ، وَالْأَخِ الصَّالِحِ"، وَلَمْ يَقِلْ: "وَالْوَلَدِ الصَّالِحِ"، كَمَا قَالَ آدَمُ وَإِبْرَاهِيمُ ، عَلَيْهِمَا السَّلَامُ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يُونُسُ، أَنْبَأَنَا ابْنُ وَهْبٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي ابْنُ لَهِيعة، عَنْ يَزِيدَ بْنِ أَبِي حَبِيبٍ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ أَنَّ إِدْرِيسَ أَقْدَمُ مِنْ نُوحٍ بَعَثَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَى قَوْمِهِ، فَأَمَرَهُمْ أَنْ يَقُولُوا: "لَا إِلَهَ إِلَّا اللَّهُ"، وَيَعْمَلُوا مَا شَاءُوا فَأَبَوْا، فَأَهْلَكَهُمُ اللَّهُ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ.

[وَمِمَّا يُؤَيِّدُ أَنَّ الْمُرَادَ بِهَذِهِ الْآيَةِ جنسُ الْأَنْبِيَاءِ، أَنَّهَا كَقَوْلِهِ تَعَالَى فِي سُورَةِ الْأَنْعَامِ: ﴿وَتِلْكَ حُجَّتُنَا آتَيْنَاهَا إِبْرَاهِيمَ عَلَى قَوْمِهِ نَرْفَعُ دَرَجَاتٍ مَنْ نَشَاءُ] إِنَّ رَبَّكَ حَكِيمٌ عَلِيمٌ * وَوَهَبْنَا لَهُ إِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ كُلا هَدَيْنَا وَنُوحًا هَدَيْنَا مِنْ قَبْلُ وَمِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِهِ دَاوُدَ وَسُلَيْمَانَ وَأَيُّوبَ وَيُوسُفَ وَمُوسَى وَهَارُونَ وَكَذَلِكَ نَجْزِي الْمُحْسِنِينَ * وَزَكَرِيَّا وَيَحْيَى وَعِيسَى وَإِلْيَاسَ كُلٌّ مِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ * وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ وَالْيَسَعَ وَيُونُسَ وَلُوطًا وَكُلا فَضَّلْنَا عَلَى الْعَالَمِينَ * وَمِنْ آبَائِهِمْ وَذُرِّيَّاتِهِمْ وَإِخْوَانِهِمْ وَاجْتَبَيْنَاهُمْ وَهَدَيْنَاهُمْ إِلَى صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ﴾ إِلَى أَنْ قَالَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ الَّذِينَ هَدَى اللَّهُ فَبِهُدَاهُمُ اقْتَدِهِ قُلْ لَا أَسْأَلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا إِنْ هُوَ إِلا ذِكْرَى لِلْعَالَمِينَ﴾ [الْأَنْعَامِ ٨٣-٩٠] وَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿مِنْهُمْ مَنْ قَصَصْنَا عَلَيْكَ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ لَمْ نَقْصُصْ عَلَيْكَ ﴾ [غَافِرٍ: ٧٨] . وَفِي صَحِيحِ الْبُخَارِيِّ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: أَنَّهُ سَأَلَ ابْنَ عَبَّاسٍ: أَفِي "ص" سَجْدَةٌ؟ قَالَ نَعَمْ، ثُمَّ تَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ الَّذِينَ هَدَى اللَّهُ فَبِهُدَاهُمُ اقْتَدِهِ﴾ ، فَنَبِيُّكُمْ مِمَّنْ أُمِر أَنْ يَقْتَدِيَ بِهِمْ، قَالَ: وَهُوَ مِنْهُمْ، يَعْنِي دَاوُدَ .

وَقَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى فِي هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ الْكَرِيمَةِ: ﴿إِذَا تُتْلَى عَلَيْهِمْ آيَاتُ الرَّحْمَنِ خَرُّوا سُجَّدًا وَبُكِيًّا﴾ أَيْ: إِذَا سَمِعُوا كَلَامَ اللَّهِ الْمُتَضَمِّنَ حُجَجه وَدَلَائِلَهُ وَبَرَاهِينَهُ، سَجَدُوا لِرَبِّهِمْ خُضُوعًا وَاسْتِكَانَةً، وَحَمْدًا وَشُكْرًا عَلَى مَا هُمْ فِيهِ مِنَ النِّعَمِ الْعَظِيمَةِ.

"والبُكِيّ": جَمْعُ بَاكٍ، فَلِهَذَا أَجْمَعَ الْعُلَمَاءُ عَلَى شَرْعِيَّةِ السُّجُودِ هَاهُنَا، اقْتِدَاءً بِهِمْ، وَاتِّبَاعًا لِمِنْوَالِهِمْ 

قَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، عَنِ الْأَعْمَشِ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، عَنْ أَبِي مَعْمَر قَالَ: قَرَأَ عُمَرُ بن الخطاب، رضي اللَّهُ عَنْهُ، سُورَةَ مَرْيَمَ، فَسَجَدَ وَقَالَ: هَذَا السُّجُودُ، فَأَيْنَ الْبُكِيُّ؟ يُرِيدُ الْبُكَاءَ.

رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، وسَقَط مِنْ رِوَايَتِهِ ذِكْرُ "أَبِي مَعْمَرٍ" فِيمَا رَأَيْتُ ، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

---

## 19:59-60 — verses 59-60 (shared commentary)

### Translation

When the Exalted mentioned the party of the fortunate ones, namely the prophets (peace be upon them) and those who followed them among those who upheld the limits and commands of God, who fulfilled God's obligations and abandoned what He forbade, He then mentioned that {a generation succeeded them after them}, meaning other generations, {who neglected the prayer}. And if they neglected it, they were even more neglectful of other obligations, for prayer is the pillar of religion and its support, and the best of the deeds of servants. They turned instead to the desires and pleasures of this world, content with worldly life and settled comfortably in it. Such people will meet ghayy, that is, loss, on the Day of Resurrection.

There is disagreement about what is meant here by "neglecting the prayer." Some said that neglecting it means abandoning it entirely. This was said by Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi, Ibn Zayd ibn Aslam, and al-Suddi, and Ibn Jarir chose this view. For this reason, some among the early and later scholars and the imams, as is well known from Imam Ahmad, and one report from al-Shafi'i, held that one who abandons prayer becomes a disbeliever, citing the hadith: "Between a servant and disbelief lies the abandonment of prayer," and another hadith: "The covenant between us and them is prayer, so whoever abandons it has disbelieved." This is not the place to elaborate on this issue.

Al-Awza'i said, from Musa ibn Sulayman, from al-Qasim ibn Mukhaymirah, regarding His saying {then a generation succeeded them after them who neglected the prayer}: he said, they only neglected its proper times, for if it meant abandonment entirely, that would be disbelief.

Waki' said, from al-Mas'udi, from al-Qasim ibn 'Abd al-Rahman and al-Hasan ibn Sa'd, from Ibn Mas'ud, that it was said to him: God mentions prayer often in the Qur'an: {those who are heedless of their prayer} and {who are constant in their prayer} and {who guard their prayer}. Ibn Mas'ud said: this refers to guarding its proper times. They said: we thought this referred only to abandonment. He said: that is disbelief.

Masruq said: no one guards the five prayers such that he is recorded among the heedless; rather, in their negligence lies ruin, and their negligence means neglecting them past their proper time.

Al-Awza'i said, from Ibrahim ibn Yazid, that 'Umar ibn 'Abd al-'Aziz recited {then a generation succeeded them after them who neglected the prayer and followed desires, so they will meet ghayy}, then said: their neglect was not abandonment of prayer, but rather they neglected its time.

Ibn Abi Najih said, from Mujahid, regarding {then a generation succeeded them after them who neglected the prayer and followed desires}: he said, this refers to the time near the establishment of the Hour, when the righteous of the nation of Muhammad ﷺ have passed away, and people mount one another openly in the streets. Ibn Jurayj related the same from Mujahid.

Jabir al-Ju'fi related from Mujahid, 'Ikrimah, and 'Ata' ibn Abi Rabah that they belong to this nation, meaning at the end of time.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] ... Mujahid said, regarding {then a generation succeeded them after them who neglected the prayer and followed desires}: they are within this nation, mounting one another in the roads like cattle and donkeys, fearing neither God in heaven nor showing shame before people on earth.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] ... Abu Sa'id al-Khudri said: I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "There will come a generation after sixty years who neglect the prayer and follow desires, so they will meet ghayy. Then there will come a generation who recite the Qur'an but it does not go past their collarbones. Three types recite the Qur'an: a believer, a hypocrite, and a transgressor." Bashir said: I asked al-Walid: who are these three? He said: the believer believes in it, the hypocrite disbelieves in it, and the transgressor eats [makes a living] by it.

Ahmad related this likewise from Abu 'Abd al-Rahman al-Muqri', with the same chain.

Ibn Abi Hatim also said: [chain] ... that 'A'isha used to send things as charity to the people of the Suffah, and would say: do not give any of it to a Berber man or woman, for I heard the Messenger of God ﷺ say: "They are the generation of whom God the Exalted said: {then a generation succeeded them after them who neglected the prayer}." This is a gharib (singular) hadith.

He also said: [chain] ... a shaykh from the people of Madinah heard Muhammad ibn Ka'b al-Qurazi say, regarding His saying {then a generation succeeded them after them}: they are the people of the West (al-Gharb), who will rule, and they are the worst of those who have ruled.

Ka'b al-Ahbar said: By God, I find the description of the hypocrites in the Book of God, Mighty and Majestic: heavy drinkers of coffee-houses' drinks, persistent abandoners of prayers, players with dice-games, sleepers through the night prayer, negligent in the early mornings, abandoners of the Friday prayer. Then he recited this verse: {then a generation succeeded them after them who neglected the prayer and followed desires, so they will meet ghayy}.

Al-Hasan al-Basri said: they left the mosques idle and clung to their farms and estates.

Abu al-Ashhab al-'Utaridi said: God the Exalted revealed to David: O David, warn and caution your companions against consuming according to desires, for hearts attached to worldly desires have their reason veiled from Me. The least of what I do to a servant among My servants, when he prefers one of his desires over Me, is that I deprive him of obedience to Me.

Imam Ahmad said: [chain] ... 'Uqbah ibn 'Amir said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "I fear two things for my nation: the Qur'an and milk. As for milk, they will follow the fertile lowlands, follow their desires, and abandon prayers. As for the Qur'an, the hypocrites will learn it and use it to argue against the believers."

He also related it from Hasan ibn Musa, from Ibn Lahi'ah, [chain] ... from 'Uqbah, with the same meaning as a raised (marfu') report; he alone transmitted it.

* *

Concerning His saying {so they will meet ghayy}: 'Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn 'Abbas: {so they will meet ghayy} means loss. Qatadah said: it means evil.

Sufyan al-Thawri, Shu'bah, and Muhammad ibn Ishaq said, from Abu Ishaq al-Sabi'i, from Abu 'Ubaydah, from 'Abdullah ibn Mas'ud, regarding {so they will meet ghayy}: he said, it is a valley in Hell, deep in its bottom, foul in its taste.

Al-A'mash said, from Ziyad, from Abu 'Iyad, regarding His saying {so they will meet ghayy}: he said, it is a valley in Hell made of pus and blood.

Imam Abu Ja'far ibn Jarir said: [chain] ... Luqman ibn 'Amir al-Khuza'i said: I came to Abu Umamah Sudayy ibn 'Ajlan al-Bahili and said, tell us a hadith you heard from the Messenger of God ﷺ. He called for food, then said: the Messenger of God ﷺ said: "If a rock weighing ten uqiyahs were thrown from the edge of Hell, it would not reach its bottom in fifty autumns, and then it would end up in ghayy and athaam." I said: what are ghayy and athaam? He said: "Two wells at the bottom of Hell, into which the pus of the people of the Fire flows. These are the two that God mentioned in His Book: {they neglected the prayer and followed desires, so they will meet ghayy}, and His saying in Surat al-Furqan: {and they do not commit adultery, and whoever does that will meet athaam (sin's penalty)}." This is a gharib hadith, and its being raised (marfu') is munkar (rejected).

* *

Concerning His saying {except one who repents, believes, and does righteous deeds}: that is, except one who turns back from abandoning prayers and following desires, for God accepts his repentance, grants him a good end, and makes him among the inheritors of the Garden of Bliss. For this reason He said: {those will enter the Garden and will not be wronged in anything}. This is because repentance cuts off what came before it. In another hadith: "One who repents from a sin is like one who has no sin." For this reason, these repentant ones are not diminished at all in the deeds they performed, nor are they held accountable for what they did before repentance such that it would be deducted from what they did after it, for that former sin has gone to waste, been left forgotten, and passed away freely, out of the generosity of the Most Generous and the forbearance of the Most Forbearing.

This exception here is like His saying in Surat al-Furqan: {And those who do not invoke another god besides God, nor kill the soul which God has forbidden except by right, nor commit adultery. And whoever does that will meet athaam. The punishment will be multiplied for him on the Day of Resurrection, and he will abide therein humiliated, except for one who repents, believes, and does righteous deeds. For those, God will replace their evil deeds with good ones, and God is Forgiving, Merciful} [al-Furqan: 68-70].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

لَمَّا ذَكَرَ تَعَالَى حزْبَ السُّعَدَاءِ، وَهُمُ الْأَنْبِيَاءُ، عَلَيْهِمُ السَّلَامُ، وَمَنِ اتَّبَعَهُمْ، مِنَ الْقَائِمِيْنَ بِحُدُودِ اللَّهِ وَأَوَامِرِهِ، الْمُؤَدِّينَ فَرَائِضَ اللَّهِ، التَّارِكِينَ لِزَوَاجِرِهِ -ذَكَرَ أَنَّهُ ﴿خَلَفَ مِنْ بَعْدِهم خَلْفٌ﴾ أَيْ: قُرُونٌ أُخَرُ، ﴿أَضَاعُوا الصَّلاةَ﴾ -وَإِذَا أَضَاعُوهَا فَهُمْ لِمَا سِوَاهَا مِنَ الْوَاجِبَاتِ أَضْيَعُ؛ لِأَنَّهَا عِمَادُ الدِّينِ وَقَوَامُهُ، وَخَيْرُ أَعْمَالِ الْعِبَادِ-وَأَقْبَلُوا عَلَى شَهَوَاتِ الدُّنْيَا وَمَلَاذِّهَا، وَرَضُوا بِالْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا وَاطْمَأَنُّوا بِهَا، فَهَؤُلَاءِ سَيَلْقَوْنَ غَيًّا، أَيْ: خَسَارًا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ.

وَقَدِ اخْتَلَفُوا فِي الْمُرَادِ بِإِضَاعَةِ الصَّلَاةِ هَاهُنَا، فَقَالَ قَائِلُونَ: الْمُرَادُ بِإِضَاعَتِهَا تَرْكُها بِالْكُلِّيَّةِ، قَالَهُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ كَعْبٍ القُرَظي، وَابْنُ زَيْدِ بْنِ أَسْلَمَ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ. وَلِهَذَا ذَهَبَ مَنْ ذَهَبَ مِنَ السَّلَفِ وَالْخَلَفِ وَالْأَئِمَّةِ كَمَا هُوَ الْمَشْهُورُ عَنِ الْإِمَامِ أَحْمَدَ، وَقَوْلٌ عَنِ الشَّافِعِيِّ إِلَى تَكْفِيرِ تَارِكِ الصَّلَاةِ، لِلْحَدِيثِ : " بَيْنَ الْعَبْدِ وَبَيْنَ الشِّرْكِ تَركُ الصَّلَاةِ" ، وَالْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: "الْعَهْدُ الَّذِي بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَهُمُ الصَّلَاةُ، فَمَنْ تَرَكَهَا فَقَدْ كَفَرَ" . وَلَيْسَ هَذَا مَحَلُّ بَسْطِ هَذِهِ الْمَسْأَلَةِ.

وَقَالَ الْأَوْزَاعِيُّ، عَنْ مُوسَى بْنِ سُلَيْمَانَ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ مُخَيمرة فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَخَلَفَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ خَلْفٌ أَضَاعُوا الصَّلاةَ﴾ ، قَالَ: إِنَّمَا أَضَاعُوا الْمَوَاقِيتَ، وَلَوْ كَانَ تَرْكًا كَانَ كُفْرًا.

وَقَالَ وَكِيعٌ، عَنِ الْمَسْعُودِيِّ، عَنِ الْقَاسِمِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، وَالْحَسَنِ بْنِ سَعْدٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ مَسْعُودٍ أَنَّهُ قِيلَ لَهُ: إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُكْثِرُ ذِكْرَ الصَّلَاةِ فِي الْقُرْآنِ: ﴿الَّذِينَ هُمْ عَنْ صَلاتِهِمْ سَاهُونَ﴾ وَ ﴿عَلَى صَلاتِهِمْ دَائِمُونَ﴾ وَ ﴿عَلَى صَلاتِهِمْ يُحَافِظُونَ﴾ ؟ قَالَ ابْنُ مَسْعُودٍ: عَلَى مَوَاقِيتِهَا. قَالُوا: مَا كُنَّا نَرَى ذَلِكَ إِلَّا عَلَى التَّرْكِ؟ قَالَ: ذَاكَ الكفر.

[و] قال مَسْرُوقٌ: لَا يُحَافِظُ أَحَدٌ عَلَى الصَّلَوَاتِ الْخَمْسِ، فَيُكْتَبُ مِنَ الْغَافِلِينَ، وَفِي إِفْرَاطِهِنَّ الْهَلَكَةُ، وَإِفْرَاطِهِنَّ: إِضَاعَتُهُنَّ عَنْ وَقْتِهِنَّ.

وَقَالَ الْأَوْزَاعِيُّ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ يَزِيدَ : أَنَّ عُمَرَ بْنَ عَبْدِ الْعَزِيزِ قَرَأَ: ﴿فَخَلَفَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ خَلْفٌ أَضَاعُوا الصَّلاةَ وَاتَّبَعُوا الشَّهَوَاتِ فَسَوْفَ يَلْقَوْنَ غَيًّا﴾ ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: لَمْ تَكُنْ إِضَاعَتُهُمْ تَرْكَهَا، وَلَكِنْ أَضَاعُوا الْوَقْتَ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي نَجِيح، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿فَخَلَفَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ خَلْفٌ أَضَاعُوا الصَّلاةَ وَاتَّبَعُوا الشَّهَوَاتِ﴾ قَالَ: عِنْدَ قِيَامِ السَّاعَةِ، وَذَهَابِ صَالِحِي أُمَّةِ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ، يَنْزُو بَعْضُهُمْ عَلَى بَعْضٍ فِي الْأَزِقَّةِ، وَكَذَا رَوَى ابْنُ جُرَيج، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، مِثْلَهُ .

وَرَوَى جَابِرٌ الجُعْفي، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ، وَعِكْرِمَةَ، وَعَطَاءِ بْنِ أَبِي رَبَاحٍ: أَنَّهُمْ مِنْ هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ، يَعْنُونَ فِي آخِرِ الزَّمَانِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي الْحَارِثُ، حَدَّثَنَا الْحَسَنُ الْأَشْيَبُ، حَدَّثَنَا شَرِيكٌ، عَنْ إِبْرَاهِيمَ بْنِ مُهَاجِرٍ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ: ﴿فَخَلَفَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ خَلْفٌ أَضَاعُوا الصَّلاةَ وَاتَّبَعُوا الشَّهَوَاتِ﴾ ، قَالَ: هُمْ فِي هَذِهِ الْأُمَّةِ ، يَتَرَاكَبُونَ تَرَاكُبَ الْأَنْعَامِ وَالْحُمُرِ فِي الطُّرُقِ، لَا يَخَافُونَ اللَّهَ فِي السَّمَاءِ، وَلَا يَسْتَحْيُونَ النَّاسَ فِي الْأَرْضِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سِنَانٍ الْوَاسِطِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ الْمُقْرِئُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَيْوَةُ، حَدَّثَنَا بَشِيرُ بْنُ أَبِي عَمْرٍو الْخَوْلَانِيُّ: أَنَّ الْوَلِيدَ بْنَ قَيْسٍ حَدَّثَهُ، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ أَبَا سَعِيدٍ الْخُدْرِيَّ يَقُولُ: سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "يَكُونُ خَلْفٌ بَعْدَ سِتِّينَ سَنَةً، أَضَاعُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَاتَّبَعُوا الشَّهَوَاتِ، فَسَوْفَ يَلْقَوْنَ غَيًّا. ثُمَّ يَكُونُ خَلْفٌ يَقْرَءُونَ الْقُرْآنَ لَا يَعْدُو تَرَاقِيَهُمْ. وَيَقْرَأُ الْقُرْآنَ ثَلَاثَةٌ: مُؤْمِنٌ، وَمُنَافِقٌ، وَفَاجِرٌ". قَالَ بَشِيرٌ : قُلْتُ لِلْوَلِيدِ: مَا هَؤُلَاءِ الثَّلَاثَةُ؟ قَالَ: الْمُؤْمِنُ مُؤْمِنٌ بِهِ، وَالْمُنَافِقُ كَافِرٌ بِهِ، وَالْفَاجِرُ يَأْكُلُ بِهِ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ أَحْمَدُ عَنْ أَبِي عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، الْمُقْرِئِ ، بِهِ 

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا إِبْرَاهِيمُ بْنُ مُوسَى، أَنْبَأَنَا عِيسَى بْنُ يُونُسَ، حَدَّثَنَا عُبَيْدُ اللَّهِ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنِ مَوْهَب ، عَنْ مَالِكٍ، عَنْ أَبِي الرِّجَالِ، أَنَّ عَائِشَةَ كَانَتْ تُرْسِلُ بِالشَّيْءِ صَدَقَةً لِأَهْلِ الصُّفَّة، وَتَقُولُ: لَا تُعْطُوا مِنْهُ بَرْبَرِيًّا وَلَا بَرْبَرِيَّةً، فَإِنِّي سَمِعْتُ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ ﷺ يَقُولُ: "هُمُ الْخَلْفُ الَّذِينَ قَالَ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: ﴿فَخَلَفَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ خَلْفٌ أَضَاعُوا الصَّلاةَ﴾ . هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ .

وَقَالَ أَيْضًا: حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّحْمَنِ بْنُ الضَّحَّاكِ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ، حَدَّثَنَا حَريز ، عَنْ شَيْخٍ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ؛ أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ مُحَمَّدَ بْنَ كَعْبٍ القُرَظِي يَقُولُ فِي قَوْلِهِ : ﴿فَخَلَفَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ خَلْفٌ﴾ الْآيَةَ، قَالَ: هُمْ أَهْلُ الْغَرْبِ ، يَمْلِكُونَ وَهُمْ شَرُّ من ملك.

وَقَالَ كَعْبُ الْأَحْبَارِ: وَاللَّهِ إِنِّي لَأَجِدُ صِفَةَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ فِي كِتَابِ اللَّهِ عَزَّ وَجَلَّ: شَرَّابِينَ لِلْقَهَوَاتِ تَرَّاكِينَ لِلصَّلَوَاتِ، لَعَّابِينَ بِالْكَعَبَاتِ، رَقَّادِينَ عَنِ الْعَتَمَاتِ، مُفَرِّطِينَ فِي الْغَدَوَاتِ، تَرَّاكِينَ لِلْجُمُعَاتِ قَالَ: ثُمَّ تَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿فَخَلَفَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِمْ خَلْفٌ أَضَاعُوا الصَّلاةَ وَاتَّبَعُوا الشَّهَوَاتِ فَسَوْفَ يَلْقَوْنَ غَيًّا﴾ .

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ الْبَصْرِيُّ: عَطَّلُوا الْمَسَاجِدَ، وَلَزِمُوا الضَّيْعَاتِ.

وَقَالَ أَبُو الْأَشْهَبِ العُطَارِدي: أَوْحَى اللَّهُ -تَعَالَى-إِلَى دَاوُدَ: يَا دَاوُدُ، حَذّر وَأَنْذِرْ أَصْحَابَكَ أَكْلَ الشَّهَوَاتِ؛ فَإِنَّ الْقُلُوبَ المعَلقة بِشَهَوَاتِ الدُّنْيَا عُقُولُهَا عَنِّي مَحْجُوبَةٌ، وَإِنَّ أَهْوَنَ مَا أَصْنَعُ بِالْعَبْدِ مِنْ عَبِيدِي إِذَا آثَرَ شَهْوَةً مِنْ شَهَوَاتِهِ عَلَيَّ أَنْ أَحْرِمَهُ طَاعَتِي.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا زَيْدُ بْنُ الْحُبَابِ حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو [السَّمْحِ] التَّمِيمِيُّ، عَنْ أَبِي قَبِيلٍ ، أَنَّهُ سَمِعَ عُقْبَةَ بْنَ عَامِرٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "إِنِّي أَخَافُ عَلَى أُمَّتِي اثْنَتَيْنِ: الْقُرْآنَ [وَاللَّبَنَ، أَمَّا اللَّبَنُ] فَيَتَّبِعُونَ الرِّيفَ، وَيَتِّبِعُونَ الشَّهَوَاتِ وَيَتْرُكُونَ الصَّلَوَاتِ، وَأَمَّا الْقُرْآنُ فَيَتَعَلَّمُهُ الْمُنَافِقُونَ، فَيُجَادِلُونَ بِهِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ" .

وَرَوَاهُ عَنْ حَسَنِ بْنِ مُوسَى، عَنِ ابْنِ لَهِيعَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو قَبِيلٍ، عَنْ عُقْبَةَ، بِهِ مَرْفُوعًا بِنَحْوِهِ تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَسَوْفَ يَلْقَوْنَ غَيًّا﴾ قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿فَسَوْفَ يَلْقَوْنَ غَيًّا﴾ أَيْ: خُسْرَانًا. وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ: شَرًّا.

وَقَالَ سُفْيَانُ الثَّوْرِيُّ، وَشُعْبَةُ، وَمُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِسْحَاقَ، عَنْ أَبِي إِسْحَاقَ السَّبيعي، عَنْ أَبِي عُبَيْدَةَ، عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ مَسْعُودٍ: ﴿فَسَوْفَ يَلْقَوْنَ غَيًّا﴾ قَالَ: وَادٍ فِي جَهَنَّمَ، بَعِيدُ الْقَعْرِ، خَبِيثُ الطَّعْمِ.

وَقَالَ الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ زِيَادٍ، عَنْ أَبِي عِيَاضٍ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿فَسَوْفَ يَلْقَوْنَ غَيًّا﴾ قَالَ: وَادٍ فِي جَهَنَّمَ مِنْ قَيْحٍ وَدَمٍ.

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَبُو جَعْفَرِ بْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنِي عَبَّاسُ بْنُ أَبِي طَالِبٍ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ زِيَادِ بْنِ زَيَّانَ، حَدَّثَنَا شَرْقِيُّ بْنُ قَطَامِيِّ، عَنْ لُقْمَانَ بْنِ عَامِرٍ الْخُزَاعِيِّ قَالَ: جِئْتُ أَبَا أُمَامَةَ صُدَيّ بْنَ عَجْلان الْبَاهِلِيَّ فَقُلْتُ: حَدِّثْنَا حَدِيثًا سَمِعْتَهُ مِنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، قَالَ: فَدَعَا بِطَعَامٍ، ثُمَّ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "لَوْ أَنَّ صَخْرَةً زِنَةَ عَشْرِ أَوَاقٍ قُذِفَ بِهَا مِنْ شَفِيرِ جَهَنَّمَ، ما بلغت قعرها خمسين خريفًا، ثُمَّ تَنْتَهِي إِلَى غَيٍّ وَآثَامٍ". قَالَ: قُلْتُ: وَمَا غَيٌّ وَآثَامٌ؟ قَالَ: "بِئْرَانِ فِي أَسْفَلِ جَهَنَّمَ، يَسِيلُ فِيهِمَا صَدِيدُ أَهْلِ النَّارِ، وَهُمَا اللَّتَانِ ذَكَرَ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ: ﴿أَضَاعُوا الصَّلاةَ وَاتَّبَعُوا الشَّهَوَاتِ فَسَوْفَ يَلْقَوْنَ غَيًّا﴾ وَقَوْلُهُ فِي الْفُرْقَانِ: ﴿وَلا يَزْنُونَ وَمَنْ يَفْعَلْ ذَلِكَ يَلْقَ أَثَامًا﴾ هَذَا حَدِيثٌ غَرِيبٌ وَرَفْعُهُ مُنْكَرٌ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِلا مَنْ تَابَ وَآمَنَ وَعَمِلَ عَمَلا صَالِحًا﴾ ، أَيْ: إِلَّا مَنْ رَجَعَ عَنْ تَرْكِ الصَّلَوَاتِ وَاتِّبَاعِ الشَّهَوَاتِ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يَقْبَلُ تَوْبَتَهُ، وَيُحْسِنُ عَاقِبَتَهُ، وَيَجْعَلُهُ مِنْ وَرَثَةِ جَنَّةِ النَّعِيمِ؛ وَلِهَذَا قَالَ: ﴿فَأُولَئِكَ يَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ وَلا يُظْلَمُونَ شَيْئًا﴾ وَذَلِكَ؛ لِأَنَّ التَّوْبَةَ تُجُبُّ مَا قَبْلَهَا، وَفِي الْحَدِيثِ الْآخَرِ: "التَّائِبَ مِنَ الذَّنْبِ كَمَنْ لَا ذَنْبَ لَهُ" ؛ وَلِهَذَا لَا يُنْقص هَؤُلَاءِ التَّائِبُونَ مِنْ أَعْمَالِهِمُ الَّتِي عَمِلُوهَا شَيْئًا، وَلَا قُوبِلُوا بِمَا عَمِلُوهُ قَبْلَهَا فَيُنْقَصُ لَهُمْ مِمَّا عَمِلُوهُ بَعْدَهَا؛ لِأَنَّ ذَلِكَ ذَهَبَ هَدَرًا وَتُرِكَ نِسْيًا، وَذَهَبَ مَجَّانا، مِنْ كَرَمِ الْكَرِيمِ، وَحِلْمِ الْحَلِيمِ.

وَهَذَا الِاسْتِثْنَاءُ هَاهُنَا كَقَوْلِهِ فِي سُورَةِ الْفُرْقَانِ: ﴿وَالَّذِينَ لَا يَدْعُونَ مَعَ اللَّهِ إِلَهًا آخَرَ وَلا يَقْتُلُونَ النَّفْسَ الَّتِي حَرَّمَ اللَّهُ إِلا بِالْحَقِّ وَلا يَزْنُونَ وَمَنْ يَفْعَلْ ذَلِكَ يَلْقَ أَثَامًا يُضَاعَفْ لَهُ الْعَذَابُ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَيَخْلُدْ فِيهِ مُهَانًا إِلا مَنْ تَابَ وَآمَنَ وَعَمِلَ عَمَلا صَالِحًا فَأُولَئِكَ يُبَدِّلُ اللَّهُ سَيِّئَاتِهِمْ حَسَنَاتٍ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا﴾ [الْفَرْقَانِ: ٦٨ -٧٠]

---

## 19:61-63 — verses 61-63 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Almighty says: the Gardens that those who repent from their sins enter are {Gardens of Eden}, meaning of permanent dwelling, {which the Most Merciful has promised His servants} while they were unseen to them, meaning: this is part of the unseen which they believe in without having seen it. That is due to the intensity of their certainty and the strength of their faith.

As for His saying, {Indeed, His promise is ever coming to pass}, this is a confirmation of the occurrence, establishment, and permanence of that. For Allah does not break His promise nor change it, as in His saying: {His promise is ever fulfilled} [al-Muzzammil: 18], meaning: it will inevitably come to be.

His saying here, {ma'tiyyan (coming to pass/arrived at)}, means: the servants are proceeding toward it, and they will come to it.

Some said: {ma'tiyyan} carries the meaning of "coming," because whatever comes to you, you have in effect come to it, just as the Arabs say: "fifty years came upon me" (atat 'alayya) and "I came upon fifty years" (ataytu 'ala khamsina sanah), both carrying the same meaning.

His saying, {They will not hear therein any vain talk}, means: in these Gardens there is no idle, worthless speech devoid of meaning, such as may be found in this world.

His saying, {except peace} is an exception of a discontinuous kind (istithna munqati'), like His saying: {They will not hear therein any vain talk or sinful speech, but only the saying: peace, peace} [al-Waqi'ah: 25-26].

His saying, {And they will have their provision therein morning and evening}, means: at times resembling the time of morning and the time of evening, not that there is actual night or day there. Rather, they are in times that succeed one another, which they recognize as passing by means of lights and radiances, as Imam Ahmad said:

[chain] Abu Hurayrah said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The first group to enter Paradise will have faces like the moon on the night it is full. They will not spit therein, nor blow their noses, nor relieve themselves. Their vessels and combs will be of gold and silver, their censers will burn aloe-wood, and their sweat will be musk. Each one of them will have two wives, so beautiful that the marrow of their shins will be visible through the flesh from beneath. There will be no disagreement or mutual hatred among them; their hearts will be as one heart, glorifying Allah morning and evening."

Both [Bukhari and Muslim] narrated it in the two Sahihs from the hadith of Ma'mar through this route.

Imam Ahmad also said: [chain] Ibn 'Abbas said: The Messenger of Allah ﷺ said: "The martyrs are upon a flashing river at the gate of Paradise, in a green dome. Their provision comes out to them from Paradise morning and evening." Ahmad alone transmitted this from this route.

Al-Dahhak said, on the authority of Ibn 'Abbas, regarding {And they will have their provision therein morning and evening}: he said: this refers to measures corresponding to night and day.

Ibn Jarir said: [chain] al-Walid ibn Muslim said: I asked Zuhayr ibn Muhammad about the words of Allah Almighty, {And they will have their provision therein morning and evening}. He said: There is no night in Paradise; they are in light forever, but they have a measure corresponding to night and day. They recognize the measure of night by the lowering of veils and the closing of doors, and they recognize the measure of day by the raising of veils and the opening of doors.

With this same chain, from al-Walid ibn Muslim, from Khulayd, from al-Hasan al-Basri, who mentioned the gates of Paradise and said: they are gates whose outer and inner sides can be seen through one another. They speak and are spoken to; a gate murmurs "open" or "close," and it does so.

Qatadah said regarding His words, {And they will have their provision therein morning and evening}: There are two periods there, a morning period and an evening period; there is neither night nor day there, but only brightness and light.

Mujahid said: there is no morning or evening there, but rather they are brought provision according to whatever they used to desire in this world.

Al-Hasan, Qatadah, and others said: among the Arabs, the most affluent among them were those who took a morning meal and an evening meal, and the Qur'an came down addressing what was already present in their minds regarding comfort and blessing, so the Almighty said: {And they will have their provision therein morning and evening}.

Ibn Mahdi said, from Hammad ibn Zayd, from Hisham, from al-Hasan, regarding {And they will have their provision therein morning and evening}: he said: the morning arrives following the evening, and the evening arrives following the morning; there is no night there.

Ibn Abi Hatim said: [chain] Abu Hurayrah reported that the Prophet ﷺ said: "There is no morning among the mornings of Paradise, and all of Paradise is mornings, except that a wife from among the wide-eyed maidens (hur al-'ayn) is brought in procession to the friend of Allah therein, the least of whom was created from saffron."

Abu Muhammad [Ibn Abi Hatim] said: this is a munkar (rejected) hadith.

As for the words of the Almighty, {That is the Paradise which We give as inheritance to those of Our servants who were righteous}, meaning: this Paradise which We have described with these magnificent attributes is what We give as inheritance to Our righteous servants, who are those obedient to Allah, Mighty and Majestic, in ease and hardship, who restrain their anger and pardon people. This is as the Almighty said at the beginning of Surat al-Mu'minun: {Certainly will the believers have succeeded. They who are during their prayer humbly submissive} up to His saying: {Those are the inheritors. Who will inherit al-Firdaws. They will abide therein eternally} [al-Mu'minun: 1-11].

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يَقُولُ تَعَالَى: الْجَنَّاتُ الَّتِي يَدْخُلُهَا التَّائِبُونَ مِنْ ذُنُوبِهِمْ، هِيَ ﴿جَنَّاتِ عَدْنٍ﴾ أَيْ: إِقَامَةٍ ﴿الَّتِي وَعَدَ الرَّحْمَنُ عِبَادَهُ﴾ بِظَهْرِ الْغَيْبِ، أَيْ: هِيَ مِنَ الْغَيْبِ الَّذِي يُؤْمِنُونَ بِهِ وَمَا رَأَوْهُ؛ وَذَلِكَ لِشِدَّةِ إِيقَانِهِمْ وَقُوَّةِ إِيمَانِهِمْ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِنَّهُ كَانَ وَعْدُهُ مَأْتِيًّا﴾ تَأْكِيدٌ لِحُصُولِ ذَلِكَ وَثُبُوتِهِ وَاسْتِقْرَارِهِ؛ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُخْلِفُ الْمِيعَادَ وَلَا يُبَدِّلُهُ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿كَانَ وَعْدُهُ مَفْعُولا﴾ [الْمُزَّمِّلِ: ١٨] أَيْ: كَائِنًا لَا مَحَالَةَ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ هَاهُنَا: ﴿مَأْتِيًّا﴾ أَيِ: الْعِبَادُ صَائِرُونَ إِلَيْهِ، وَسَيَأْتُونَهُ.

وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ قَالَ: ﴿مَأْتِيًّا﴾ بِمَعْنَى: آتِيًا؛ لِأَنَّ كُلَّ مَا أَتَاكَ فَقَدْ أَتَيْتَهُ، كَمَا تَقُولُ الْعَرَبُ: أَتَتْ عَلَيَّ خَمْسُونَ سَنَةً، وَأَتَيْتُ عَلَى خَمْسِينَ سَنَةً، كلاهما بمعنى [واحد] وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَا يَسْمَعُونَ فِيهَا لَغْوًا﴾ أَيْ: هَذِهِ الْجَنَّاتُ لَيْسَ فِيهَا كَلَامٌ سَاقِطٌ تَافِهٌ لَا مَعْنًى لَهُ، كَمَا قَدْ يُوجَدُ فِي الدُّنْيَا.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿إِلا سَلامًا﴾ اسْتِثْنَاءٌ مُنْقَطِعٌ، كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿لَا يَسْمَعُونَ فِيهَا لَغْوًا وَلا تَأْثِيمًا إِلا قِيلا سَلامًا سَلامًا﴾ [الْوَاقِعَةِ: ٢٥، ٢٦] 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَلَهُمْ رِزْقُهُمْ فِيهَا بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيًّا﴾ أَيْ: فِي مِثْلِ وَقْتِ البُكُرات وَوَقْتِ العَشيّات، لَا أَنَّ هُنَاكَ لَيْلًا أَوْ نَهَارًا وَلَكِنَّهُمْ فِي أَوْقَاتٍ تَتَعَاقَبُ، يَعْرِفُونَ مُضِيَّهَا بِأَضْوَاءٍ وَأَنْوَارٍ، كَمَا قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ:

حَدَّثَنَا عَبْدُ الرَّزَّاقِ، حَدَّثَنَا معْمَر، عَنْ هَمَّام، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَوَّلُ زُمْرَة تَلِجُ الْجَنَّةَ صُورهم عَلَى صُورَةِ الْقَمَرِ لَيْلَةَ الْبَدْرِ، لَا يبصُقون فِيهَا، وَلَا يَتَمَخَّطُونَ فِيهَا، وَلَا يَتَغَوّطون، آنِيَتُهُمْ وَأَمْشَاطُهُمُ الذَّهَبُ وَالْفِضَّةُ، وَمُجَامِرُهُمُ الألْوّة، ورَشْحُهم الْمِسْكُ، وَلِكُلِّ وَاحِدٍ مِنْهُمْ زَوْجَتَانِ، يَرَى مُخّ سَاقَيْهِمَا مِنْ وَرَاءِ اللَّحْمِ؛ مِنَ الْحُسْنِ، لَا اخْتِلَافَ بَيْنِهِمْ وَلَا تَبَاغُضَ، قُلُوبُهُمْ عَلَى قَلْبٍ وَاحِدٍ، يُسَبِّحُونَ اللَّهَ بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيًّا".

أَخْرَجَاهُ فِي الصَّحِيحَيْنِ مِنْ حَدِيثِ مَعْمَرٍ بِهِ 

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَعْقُوبُ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبِي، عَنِ ابْنِ إِسْحَاقَ، حَدَّثَنِي الْحَارِثُ بْنُ فُضَيْلٍ الْأَنْصَارِيُّ، عَنْ مَحْمُودِ بْنِ لَبِيدٍ الْأَنْصَارِيِّ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "الشُّهَدَاءُ عَلَى بَارِقِ نَهْرٍ بِبَابِ الْجَنَّةِ، فِي قُبَّةٍ خَضْرَاءَ، يَخْرُجُ عَلَيْهِمْ رِزْقُهُمْ مِنَ الْجَنَّةِ بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيًّا" تَفَرَّدَ بِهِ أَحْمَدُ مِنْ هَذَا الْوَجْهِ.

وَقَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: ﴿وَلَهُمْ رِزْقُهُمْ فِيهَا بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: مَقَادِيرُ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ سَهْمٍ، حَدَّثَنَا الْوَلِيدُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ قَالَ: سَأَلْتُ زُهَيْرَ بْنَ مُحَمَّدٍ، عَنْ قَوْلِ اللَّهِ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَهُمْ رِزْقُهُمْ فِيهَا بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: لَيْسَ فِي الْجَنَّةِ لَيْلٌ، هُمْ فِي نُورٍ أَبَدًا، وَلَهُمْ مِقْدَارُ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ، يَعْرِفُونَ مِقْدَارَ اللَّيْلِ بِإِرْخَاءِ الْحُجُبِ وَإِغْلَاقِ الْأَبْوَابِ، وَيَعْرِفُونَ مِقْدَارَ النَّهَارِ بِرَفْعِ الْحُجُبِ، وَبِفَتْحِ الْأَبْوَابِ.

وَبِهَذَا الْإِسْنَادِ عَنِ الْوَلِيدِ بْنِ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ خُلَيْد، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ الْبَصْرِيِّ، وَذَكَرَ أَبْوَابَ الْجَنَّةِ، فَقَالَ: أَبْوَابٌ يُرى ظَاهِرُهَا مِنْ بَاطِنِهَا، فَتُكَلِّمُ وَتُكَلَّمُ، فَتُهَمْهِم انفتحي انغلقي، فتفعل.

وَقَالَ قَتَادَةُ فِي قَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَلَهُمْ رِزْقُهُمْ فِيهَا بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيًّا﴾ : فِيهَا سَاعَتَانِ: بَكَرَةٌ وَعَشِيٌّ: لَيْسَ ثَمَّ لَيْلٌ وَلَا نَهَارٌ، وَإِنَّمَا هُوَ ضَوْءٌ وَنُورٌ.

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ لَيْسَ [فِيهَا] بُكْرَةٌ وَلَا عَشِيٌّ، وَلَكِنْ يُؤتون بِهِ عَلَى مَا كَانُوا يَشْتَهُونَ فِي الدُّنْيَا.

وَقَالَ الْحَسَنُ، وقَتَادَةُ، وَغَيْرُهُمَا: كَانَتِ الْعَرَبُ، الأنْعَم فِيهِمْ، مَنْ يَتَغَدَّى وَيَتَعَشَّى، وَنَزَلَ الْقُرْآنُ عَلَى مَا فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ مِنَ النَّعِيمِ، فَقَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَلَهُمْ رِزْقُهُمْ فِيهَا بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيًّا﴾

وَقَالَ ابْنِ مَهْدِيٍّ، عَنْ حَمَّادِ بْنِ زَيْدٍ، عَنْ هِشَامٍ، عَنِ الْحَسَنِ: ﴿وَلَهُمْ رِزْقُهُمْ فِيهَا بُكْرَةً وَعَشِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: الْبُكُورُ يَرِدُ عَلَى الْعَشِيِّ، وَالْعَشِيُّ يَرِدُ عَلَى الْبُكُورِ، لَيْسَ فِيهَا لَيْلٌ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَيْنِ، حَدَّثَنَا سَلِيمُ بْنُ مَنْصُورِ بْنِ عَمَّارٍ، حَدَّثَنِي أَبِي، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ زِيَادٍ قَاضِي أَهْلِ شَمْشَاط عَنْ عَبْدِ اللَّهِ بْنِ جَرِيرٍ عَنْ أَبِي سَلَمَةَ بْنِ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ، عَنْ أَبِي هُرَيْرَةَ، عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ قَالَ: "مَا مِنْ غَدَاةٍ مِنْ غَدَوَاتِ الْجَنَّةِ، وَكُلُّ الْجَنَّةِ غَدَوَاتٌ، إِلَّا أَنَّهُ يُزَفُّ إِلَى وَلِيِّ اللَّهِ فِيهَا زَوْجَةٌ مِنَ الْحَوَرِ الْعَيْنِ، أَدْنَاهُنَّ الَّتِي خُلِقَتْ مِنَ الزَّعْفَرَانِ" 

قَالَ أَبُو مُحَمَّدٍ: هَذَا حَدِيثٌ مُنْكَرٌ.

[وَقَوْلُهُ تَعَالَى] ﴿تِلْكَ الْجَنَّةُ الَّتِي نُورِثُ مِنْ عِبَادِنَا مَنْ كَانَ تَقِيًّا﴾ أَيْ: هَذِهِ الْجَنَّةُ الَّتِي وَصَفْنَا بِهَذِهِ الصِّفَاتِ الْعَظِيمَةِ هِيَ الَّتِي نُورِثُهَا عِبَادَنَا الْمُتَّقِينَ، وَهُمُ الْمُطِيعُونَ لِلَّهِ -عَزَّ وَجَلَّ-فِي السَّرَّاءِ وَالضَّرَّاءِ، وَالْكَاظِمُونَ الْغَيْظَ وَالْعَافُونَ عَنِ النَّاسِ، وَكَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى فِي أَوَّلِ سُورَةِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ: ﴿قَدْ أَفْلَحَ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ. الَّذِينَ هُمْ فِي صَلاتِهِمْ خَاشِعُونَ﴾ إِلَى أَنْ قَالَ: ﴿أُولَئِكَ هُمُ الْوَارِثُونَ الَّذِينَ يَرِثُونَ الْفِرْدَوْسَ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ﴾ [الْمُؤْمِنُونَ: ١-١١]

---

## 19:64-65 — verses 64-65 (shared commentary)

### Translation

Imam Ahmad said: Ya'la and Waki' related to us, saying, Umar ibn Dharr related to us, from his father, from Sa'id ibn Jubayr, from Ibn Abbas, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to Gabriel, "What prevents you from visiting us more than you do?" He said: then {And we do not descend except by the command of your Lord} was revealed, to the end of the verse.

Al-Bukhari alone reported this, narrating it in his commentary on this verse from Abu Nu'aym, from Umar ibn Dharr, with this chain. Ibn Abi Hatim and Ibn Jarir also reported it, from the hadith of Umar ibn Dharr with this chain, and in their versions there is an addition at the end of the hadith, namely that this was the answer given to Muhammad ﷺ.

Al-Awfi said, from Ibn Abbas: Gabriel withheld himself from the Messenger of Allah ﷺ, and the Messenger of Allah ﷺ felt distress and sorrow over this. Then Gabriel came to him and said: O Muhammad, {And we do not descend except by the command of your Lord. To Him belongs what is before us and what is behind us and what is between that, and your Lord is never forgetful}.

Mujahid said: Gabriel remained away from Muhammad ﷺ for twelve nights, and they say [it was shortened to a smaller number]. When he came to him, he said: "O Gabriel, you have delayed toward me so long that the polytheists have begun to think all sorts of things." Then {And we do not descend except by the command of your Lord [To Him belongs what is before us and what is behind us and what is between that] and your Lord is never forgetful} was revealed. He said: this verse is like the one in Surah al-Duha.

Similarly, al-Dahhak ibn Muzahim, Qatadah, al-Suddi, and others said that it was revealed regarding Gabriel's withholding himself.

Al-Hakam ibn Aban said, from Ikrimah: Gabriel delayed his descent to the Messenger of Allah ﷺ for forty days, then he descended, and the Prophet ﷺ said to him, "You did not come down until I longed for you." Gabriel said to him: rather, I longed for you even more, but I am one who is commanded. Then it was revealed to Gabriel that he should say to him: {And we do not descend except by the command of your Lord}, the verse. Ibn Abi Hatim, may Allah have mercy on him, reported it, and it is gharib (singular, a solitary report).

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Ahmad ibn Sinan related to us, Abu Mu'awiyah related to us, al-A'mash related to us, from Mujahid, who said: the messengers (angels) delayed in coming to the Prophet ﷺ, then Gabriel came to him, and he said to him: "What kept you back, O Gabriel?" Gabriel said to him: how could we come to you when you do not cut your nails, do not clean your finger joints, do not trim your mustaches, and do not use the tooth-stick? Then he recited: {And we do not descend except by the command of your Lord}, to the end of the verse.

Al-Tabarani said: Abu Amir al-Nahwi related to us, Muhammad ibn Ibrahim al-Suri related to us, Sulayman ibn Abd al-Rahman [al-Dimashqi] related to us, Isma'il ibn Ayyash related to us, Tha'labah ibn Muslim informed me, from Abu Ka'b, the client of Ibn Abbas, from Ibn Abbas, from the Prophet ﷺ: that Gabriel delayed with him, and he mentioned that to him, so he said: "And how could it be otherwise, when you do not use the tooth-stick, do not trim your nails, do not cut your mustaches, and do not clean your finger joints?"

Imam Ahmad likewise reported it, from Abu al-Yaman, from Isma'il ibn Ayyash, with this chain, similarly.

Imam Ahmad said: Sayyar related to us, Ja'far ibn Sulayman related to us, al-Mughirah ibn Habib, the son-in-law of Malik ibn Dinar, related to us, an elder from the people of Madinah related to me, from Umm Salamah, who said: the Messenger of Allah ﷺ said to me: "Set the gathering place in order for us, for an angel is about to descend to the earth who has never descended to it before."

Regarding His saying, {To Him belongs what is before us and what is behind us}: it is said that what is meant by "what is before us" is the affair of this world, and "what is behind us" is the affair of the hereafter, and {what is between that} is what lies between the two blowings of the trumpet. This is the saying of Abu al-Aliyah, Ikrimah, Mujahid, and Sa'id ibn Jubayr, and of Qatadah in one report from him and Ibn Abbas, and of al-Suddi and al-Rabi' ibn Anas.

It is also said: {what is before us} is what we face of the affair of the hereafter, and {what is behind us} means what has passed of this world, and {what is between that} means what is between this world and the hereafter. Something similar is reported from Ibn Abbas, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, al-Dahhak, Qatadah, Ibn Jurayj, and al-Thawri. Ibn Jarir also chose this view, and Allah knows best.

Regarding His saying, {and your Lord is never forgetful}: Mujahid [and al-Suddi] said its meaning is: your Lord has not forgotten you.

It was mentioned earlier from him that this verse is like His saying: {By the morning brightness, and by the night when it grows still, your Lord has not forsaken you, nor does He hate you} [al-Duha 93:1-3].

Ibn Abi Hatim said: Yazid ibn Muhammad ibn Abd al-Samad al-Dimashqi related to us, Muhammad ibn Uthman, that is, Abu al-Jumahir, related to us, Isma'il ibn Ayyash related to us, Asim ibn Raja' ibn Haywah related to us, from his father, from Abu al-Darda, raising it (to the Prophet ﷺ), who said: "What Allah has made lawful in His Book is lawful, and what He has made unlawful is unlawful, and what He has remained silent about is a matter of pardon, so accept from Allah His pardon, for Allah would never forget anything." Then he recited this verse: {and your Lord is never forgetful}.

Regarding His saying, {Lord of the heavens and the earth and what is between them} that is, the Creator of that and its Manager, the Ruler over it and the Disposer whose ruling none can overturn, {so worship Him and be steadfast in worship of Him. Do you know of any equal to Him?}: Ali ibn Abi Talhah said, from Ibn Abbas: do you know of any likeness or resemblance to the Lord.

Similarly Mujahid, Sa'id ibn Jubayr, Qatadah, Ibn Jurayj, and others said.

Ikrimah said, from Ibn Abbas: no one is named al-Rahman (the Most Merciful) besides Him, blessed and exalted is He, and holy is His name.

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

قَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا يَعْلى وَوَكِيعٌ قَالَا حَدَّثَنَا عُمَرُ بْنُ ذَرّ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ سَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْر، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ قَالَ: قَالَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ لِجِبْرِيلَ: "مَا يَمْنَعُكَ أَنْ تَزُورَنَا أَكْثَرَ مِمَّا تَزُورُنَا؟ " قَالَ: فَنَزَلَتْ ﴿وَمَا نَتَنزلُ إِلا بِأَمْرِ رَبِّكَ﴾ إِلَى آخَرِ الْآيَةِ.

انْفَرَدَ بِإِخْرَاجِهِ الْبُخَارِيُّ، فَرَوَاهُ عِنْدَ تَفْسِيرِ هَذِهِ الْآيَةِ عَنْ أَبِي نُعَيْمٍ، عَنْ عُمَرَ بْنِ ذَرٍّ بِهِ. وَرَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ وَابْنُ جَرِيرٍ، مِنْ حَدِيثِ عُمَرَ بْنِ ذَرٍّ بِهِ وَعِنْدَهُمَا زِيَادَةٌ فِي آخِرِ الْحَدِيثِ، فكان ذَلِكَ الْجَوَابُ لِمُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ.

وَقَالَ العَوْفي عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: احْتَبَسَ جِبْرِيلُ عَنْ رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ، فَوَجَدَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ مِنْ ذَلِكَ وحَزَن، فَأَتَاهُ جِبْرِيلُ وَقَالَ: يَا مُحَمَّدُ، ﴿وَمَا نَتَنزلُ إِلا بِأَمْرِ رَبِّكَ لَهُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِينَا وَمَا خَلْفَنَا وَمَا بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ وَمَا كَانَ رَبُّكَ نَسِيًّا﴾

وَقَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ: لَبِثَ جِبْرِيلُ عَنْ مُحَمَّدٍ ﷺ اثْنَتَيْ عَشْرَةَ لَيْلَةً، وَيَقُولُونَ [قُلِيَ] فَلَمَّا جَاءَهُ قَالَ: يَا جِبْرِيلُ لَقَدْ رِثْتَ عَلَيَّ حَتَّى ظَنَّ الْمُشْرِكُونَ كُلَّ ظَنٍّ. فَنَزَلَتْ: ﴿وَمَا نَتَنزلُ إِلا بِأَمْرِ رَبِّكَ [لَهُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِينَا وَمَا خَلْفَنَا وَمَا بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ] وَمَا كَانَ رَبُّكَ نَسِيًّا﴾ قَالَ: وَهَذِهِ الْآيَةُ كَالَّتِي فِي الضُّحَى.

وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ الضَّحَّاكُ بْنُ مُزَاحم، وقَتَادَةُ، وَالسُّدِّيُّ، وَغَيْرُ وَاحِدٍ: إِنَّهَا نَزَلَتْ فِي احْتِبَاسِ جِبْرِيلَ.

وَقَالَ الْحَكَمُ بْنُ أَبَانَ، عَنْ عِكْرِمَةَ قَالَ: أَبْطَأَ جِبْرِيلُ النُّزُولَ عَلَى رَسُولِ اللَّهِ ﷺ أَرْبَعِينَ يَوْمًا، ثُمَّ نَزَلَ، فَقَالَ لَهُ النَّبِيُّ ﷺ: "مَا نَزَلْتَ حَتَّى اشْتَقْتُ إِلَيْكَ" فَقَالَ لَهُ جِبْرِيلُ: بَلْ أَنَا كُنْتُ إِلَيْكَ أَشْوَقُ، وَلَكِنِّي مَأْمُورٌ، فأوحِيَ إِلَى جِبْرِيلَ أَنْ قُلْ لَهُ: ﴿وَمَا نَتَنزلُ إِلا بِأَمْرِ رَبِّكَ﴾ الْآيَةَ. رَوَاهُ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ، رَحِمَهُ اللَّهُ، وَهُوَ غَرِيبٌ.

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا أَحْمَدُ بْنُ سِنَانٍ، حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو مُعَاوِيَةَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْأَعْمَشُ، عَنْ مُجَاهِدٍ قَالَ: أَبْطَأَتِ الرسلُ عَلَى النَّبِيِّ ﷺ، ثُمَّ أَتَاهُ جِبْرِيلُ فَقَالَ لَهُ: مَا حَبَسَكَ يَا جِبْرِيلُ؟ فَقَالَ لَهُ جِبْرِيلُ: وَكَيْفَ نَأْتِيكُمْ وَأَنْتُمْ لَا تَقُصُّونَ أَظْفَارَكُمْ، وَلَا تُنْقُون بَرَاجِمَكُمْ، وَلَا تَأْخُذُونَ شَوَارِبَكُمْ، وَلَا تَسْتَاكُونَ؟ ثُمَّ قَرَأَ: ﴿وَمَا نَتَنزلُ إِلا بِأَمْرِ رَبِّكَ﴾ إِلَى آخِرِ الْآيَةِ.

وَقَدْ قَالَ الطَّبَرَانِيُّ: حَدَّثَنَا أَبُو عَامِرٍ النَّحْوِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الصُّورِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا سُلَيْمَانُ بْنُ عَبْدِ الرَّحْمَنِ [الدِّمَشْقِيُّ] حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ عَيَّاشٍ، أَخْبَرَنِي ثَعْلَبَةُ بْنُ مُسْلِمٍ، عَنْ أَبِي كَعْبٍ مَوْلَى ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ عَنِ النَّبِيِّ ﷺ: أَنَّ جِبْرِيلَ أَبْطَأَ عَلَيْهِ، فَذَكَرَ ذَلِكَ لَهُ فَقَالَ: وَكَيْفَ وَأَنْتُمْ لَا تَسْتَنّون، وَلَا تُقَلّمُون أَظْفَارَكُمْ، وَلَا تَقُصُّونَ شَوَارِبَكُمْ، وَلَا تُنْقُون رَوُاجِبَكُمْ.

وَهَكَذَا رَوَاهُ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ، عَنْ أَبِي الْيَمَانِ، عَنْ إِسْمَاعِيلَ بْنِ عَيَّاشٍ، بِهِ نَحْوَهُ .

وَقَالَ الْإِمَامُ أَحْمَدُ: حَدَّثَنَا سَيَّار، حَدَّثَنَا جَعْفَرُ بْنُ سُلَيْمَانَ، حَدَّثَنَا الْمُغِيرَةُ بْنُ حَبِيبٍ -[خَتَنُ] مَالِكِ بْنِ دِينَارٍ-حَدَّثَنِي شَيْخٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْمَدِينَةِ، عَنْ أُمِّ سَلَمَةَ قَالَتْ: قَالَ لِي رَسُولُ اللَّهِ ﷺ: "أَصْلِحِي لَنَا الْمَجْلِسَ، فَإِنَّهُ يَنْزِلُ مَلَكٌ إِلَى الْأَرْضِ، لَمْ يَنْزِلْ إِلَيْهَا قَطُّ" 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿لَهُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِينَا وَمَا خَلْفَنَا﴾ قِيلَ: الْمُرَادُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِينَا: أَمْرُ الدُّنْيَا، وَمَا خَلْفَنَا: أَمْرُ الْآخِرَةِ، ﴿وَمَا بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ﴾ مَا بَيْنَ النَّفْخَتَيْنِ. هَذَا قَوْلُ أَبِي العالية، وعكرمة، ومجاهد، وسعيد بن جُبَيْرٍ. وَقَتَادَةَ، فِي رِوَايَةٍ عَنْهُمَا، وَالسُّدِّيِّ، وَالرَّبِيعِ بْنِ أَنَسٍ.

وَقِيلَ: ﴿مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِينَا﴾ مَا نَسْتَقْبِلُ مِنْ أَمْرِ الْآخِرَةِ، ﴿وَمَا خَلْفَنَا﴾ أَيْ: مَا مَضَى مِنَ الدُّنْيَا، ﴿وَمَا بَيْنَ ذَلِكَ﴾ أَيْ: مَا بَيْنَ الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ. يُرْوَى نَحْوُهُ عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ، وَسَعِيدِ بْنِ جُبَيْرٍ، وَالضَّحَّاكِ، وقَتَادَةَ، وَابْنِ جُرَيْجٍ، وَالثَّوْرِيِّ. وَاخْتَارَهُ ابْنُ جَرِيرٍ أَيْضًا، وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ.

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ رَبُّكَ نَسِيًّا﴾ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ [والسُّدِّيّ] مَعْنَاهُ: مَا نَسِيَكَ رَبُّكَ.

وَقَدْ تَقَدَّمَ عَنْهُ أَنَّ هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَالضُّحَى وَاللَّيْلِ إِذَا سَجَى مَا وَدَّعَكَ رَبُّكَ وَمَا قَلَى﴾ [الضُّحَى: ١-٣]

وَقَالَ ابْنُ أَبِي حَاتِمٍ: حَدَّثَنَا يَزِيدُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَبْدِ الصَّمَدِ الدِّمَشْقِيُّ، حَدَّثَنَا مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عُثْمَانَ -يَعْنِي أَبَا الْجُمَاهِرِ -حَدَّثَنَا إِسْمَاعِيلُ بْنُ عَيَّاشٍ، حَدَّثَنَا عَاصِمُ بْنُ رَجَاءِ بْنِ حَيْوَةَ، عَنْ أَبِيهِ، عَنْ أَبِي الدَّرْدَاءِ يَرْفَعُهُ قَالَ: "مَا أَحَلَّ اللَّهُ فِي كِتَابِهِ فَهُوَ حَلَالٌ وَمَا حَرَّمَ فَهُوَ حَرَامٌ وَمَا سَكَتَ [عَنْهُ] فَهُوَ عَافِيَةٌ، فَاقْبَلُوا مِنَ اللَّهِ عَافِيَتَهُ، فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَمْ يَكُنْ لِيَنْسَى شَيْئًا" ثُمَّ تَلَا هَذِهِ الْآيَةَ: ﴿وَمَا كَانَ رَبُّكَ نَسِيًّا﴾ 

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿رَبُّ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالأرْضِ وَمَا بَيْنَهُمَا﴾ [أَيْ: خَالِقٌ ذَلِكَ وَمُدَبِّرُهُ، وَالْحَاكِمُ فِيهِ وَالْمُتَصَرِّفُ الَّذِي لَا مُعَقِّبَ لِحُكْمِهِ، ﴿فَاعْبُدْهُ وَاصْطَبِرْ لِعِبَادَتِهِ] هَلْ تَعْلَمُ لَهُ سَمِيًّا﴾ : قَالَ عَلِيُّ بْنُ أَبِي طَلْحَةَ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: هَلْ تَعْلَمُ لِلرَّبِّ مَثَلًا أَوْ شَبَهًا.

وَكَذَلِكَ قَالَ مُجَاهِدٌ، وَسَعِيدُ بْنُ جُبَيْرٍ، وقَتَادَةُ، وَابْنُ جُرَيْجٍ وَغَيْرُهُمْ.

وَقَالَ عِكْرِمَةُ، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: لَيْسَ أَحَدٌ يُسَمَّى الرَّحْمَنَ غَيْرَهُ تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى، وَتَقَدَّسَ اسْمُهُ.

---

## 19:66-70 — verses 66-70 (shared commentary)

### Translation

The Exalted informs us about man, that he is astonished and thinks it far-fetched that he could be brought back after his death, just as He, the Exalted, said: {And if you are astonished, then astonishing indeed is their saying: "When we are dust, shall we truly be raised in a new creation?"} [al-Ra'd: 5], and He said: {Does man not see that We created him from a sperm-drop, yet he is an open disputant? And he has struck for Us a similitude and forgotten his own creation, saying: "Who will give life to bones when they have decayed?" Say: "He will give them life who produced them the first time, and He is knowing of every creation."} [Ya-Sin: 77-79]. And He said here: {And man says: "When I am dead, will I indeed be brought forth alive?" Does man not remember that We created him before, when he was nothing?} He, the Exalted, draws proof for the return (resurrection) from the original bringing into being. That is, that He, the Exalted, [indeed] created man when he was nothing, so will He not bring him back again now that he has become something? Just as He, the Exalted, said: {And He is the One who begins creation, then repeats it, and that is easier for Him} [al-Rum: 27]. And in the authentic hadith: "Allah, the Exalted, says: 'The son of Adam has denied Me, though he had no right to deny Me, and the son of Adam has insulted Me, though he had no right to insult Me. As for his denial of Me, it is his saying: He will never bring me back as He originated me, and the first creation is no easier for Me than the last. And as for his insult to Me, it is his saying: Indeed I have a son, while I am al-Ahad (the One), al-Samad (the Self-Sufficient Master, free of all need, upon whom all depend), who has not begotten and was not begotten, and there is none equal to Him.'"

And His saying: {So by your Lord, We will surely gather them and the devils}. The Lord, blessed and exalted is He, has sworn by His own noble Self that He will most certainly gather them all together, along with their devils whom they used to worship besides Allah, {then We will surely bring them, kneeling, around Hell}.

Al-'Awfi said, from Ibn 'Abbas: meaning, seated, as in His saying: {And you will see every nation kneeling} [al-Jathiyah: 28].

Al-Suddi said regarding His saying: {then We will surely bring them, kneeling, around Hell}: meaning, standing. And it has been related from Murrah, from Ibn Mas'ud, [likewise].

And His saying: {Then We will surely draw out from every sect}, meaning from every nation, as Mujahid said, {whichever of them was most obstinate in rebellion against the Most Merciful}.

Al-Thawri said, from ['Ali ibn al-Aqmar], from Abu al-Ahwas, from Ibn Mas'ud, who said: He will hold back the first for the sake of the last, until when the full number is complete, He will bring them all together, then He will begin with the greatest, then the next greatest in crime. This is the meaning of His saying: {Then We will surely draw out from every sect whichever of them was most obstinate in rebellion against the Most Merciful}.

And Qatadah said concerning {Then We will surely draw out from every sect whichever of them was most obstinate in rebellion against the Most Merciful}: he said, meaning We will draw out from the followers of every religion their leaders and their chiefs in evil. And Ibn Jurayj and more than one of the predecessors said the same. This is like His saying, the Exalted: {Until, when they have all overtaken one another therein, the last of them will say of the first of them: "Our Lord, these led us astray, so give them a double portion of the punishment of the Fire." He will say: "For each is a double portion, but you do not know." And the first of them will say to the last of them: "Then you had no advantage over us, so taste the punishment for what you used to earn."} [al-A'raf: 38-39].

And His saying: {Then indeed We know best those most worthy of being burned therein}. "Then" here connects one statement to another statement, and what is meant is that He, the Exalted, knows best which of His servants deserve to be burned in the fire of Hell and to remain in it forever, and which deserve a doubled punishment, just as He said in the preceding verse: {He will say: "For each is a double portion, but you do not know."}

### Source (Arabic) — review against this

يُخْبِرُ تَعَالَى عَنِ الْإِنْسَانِ أَنَّهُ يَتَعَجَّبُ وَيَسْتَبْعِدُ إِعَادَتَهُ بَعْدَ مَوْتِهِ، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَإِنْ تَعْجَبْ فَعَجَبٌ قَوْلُهُمْ أَئِذَا كُنَّا تُرَابًا أَئِنَّا لَفِي خَلْقٍ جَدِيدٍ﴾ [الرعد: ٥] ، وَقَالَ: ﴿أَوَلَمْ يَرَ الإنْسَانُ أَنَّا خَلَقْنَاهُ مِنْ نُطْفَةٍ فَإِذَا هُوَ خَصِيمٌ مُبِينٌ * وَضَرَبَ لَنَا مَثَلا وَنَسِيَ خَلْقَهُ قَالَ مَنْ يُحْيِي الْعِظَامَ وَهِيَ رَمِيمٌ * قُلْ يُحْيِيهَا الَّذِي أَنْشَأَهَا أَوَّلَ مَرَّةٍ وَهُوَ بِكُلِّ خَلْقٍ عَلِيمٌ﴾ [يس: ٧٧-٧٩] ، وَقَالَ هَاهُنَا: ﴿وَيَقُولُ الإنْسَانُ أَئِذَا مَا مِتُّ لَسَوْفَ أُخْرَجُ حَيًّا * أَوَلا يَذْكُرُ الإنْسَانُ أَنَّا خَلَقْنَاهُ مِنْ قَبْلُ وَلَمْ يَكُ شَيْئًا﴾ يَسْتَدِلُّ، تَعَالَى، بِالْبَدَاءَةِ عَلَى الْإِعَادَةِ، يَعْنِي أَنَّهُ، تَعَالَى [قَدْ] خَلَقَ الْإِنْسَانَ وَلَمْ يَكُ شَيْئًا، أَفَلَا يُعِيدُهُ وَقَدْ صَارَ شَيْئًا، كَمَا قَالَ تَعَالَى: ﴿وَهُوَ الَّذِي يَبْدَأُ الْخَلْقَ ثُمَّ يُعِيدُهُ وَهُوَ أَهْوَنُ عَلَيْهِ﴾ [الرُّومِ: ٢٧] ، وَفِي الصَّحِيحِ: "يَقُولُ اللَّهُ تَعَالَى: كَذَّبَنِي ابْنُ آدَمَ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ أَنْ يُكَذِّبَنِي، وَآذَانِي ابْنُ آدَمَ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ أَنْ يُؤْذِيَنِي، أَمَّا تَكْذِيبُهُ إِيَّايَ فَقَوْلُهُ: لَنْ يُعِيدَنِي كَمَا بَدَأَنِي، وَلَيْسَ أَوَّلُ الْخَلْقِ بِأَهْوَنَ عَلِيَّ مِنْ آخِرِهِ، وَأَمَّا أَذَاهُ إِيَّايَ فَقَوْلُهُ: إِنَّ لِي وَلَدًا، وَأَنَا الْأَحَدُ الصَّمَدُ، الَّذِي لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌ" .

* *

وَقَوْلُهُ: ﴿فَوَرَبِّكَ لَنَحْشُرَنَّهُمْ وَالشَّيَاطِينَ﴾ أَقْسَمَ الرَّبُّ، تَبَارَكَ وَتَعَالَى، بِنَفْسِهِ الْكَرِيمَةِ، أَنَّهُ لَا بُدَّ أَنْ يَحْشُرَهُمْ جَمِيعًا وَشَيَاطِينَهُمُ الَّذِينَ كَانُوا يَعْبُدُونَ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ، ﴿ثُمَّ لَنُحْضِرَنَّهُمْ حَوْلَ جَهَنَّمَ جِثِيًّا﴾ .

قَالَ العَوْفي، عَنِ ابْنِ عَبَّاسٍ: يَعْنِي: قُعُودًا كَقَوْلِهِ: ﴿وَتَرَى كُلَّ أُمَّةٍ جَاثِيَةً﴾ [الْجَاثِيَةِ: ٢٨] .
